A Bit Much	<b>Bengali:</b> একটু বেশি, অত্যধিক<br><b>English:</b> Too much; excessive<br><b>Example:</b> His constant complaining is a bit much - we get it, you're unhappy.	
A Bite at The Cherry	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি ভাল সুযোগ যা সবার জন্য উপলব্ধ নয়<br><b>English:</b> A good opportunity that is not available to everyone<br><b>Example:</b> Getting an interview at Google is a bite at the cherry that few candidates receive.	
A Busy Bee	<b>Bengali:</b> একজন ব্যস্ত, সক্রিয় ব্যক্তি যে দ্রুত এক কাজ থেকে আরেক কাজে চলে যায়<br><b>English:</b> A busy, active person who moves quickly from one task to another<br><b>Example:</b> Sarah is such a busy bee - she's already finished three projects this week.	
A Cat Has Nine Lives	<b>Bengali:</b> বিড়ালের নয়টি জীবন আছে, বিপদ থেকে বেঁচে যাওয়ার ক্ষমতা<br><b>English:</b> The ability to survive danger or bounce back from misfortune<br><b>Example:</b> After surviving three car accidents, John jokes that he has nine lives like a cat.	
A Cat Nap	<b>Bengali:</b> দিনের বেলা একটি ছোট ঘুম<br><b>English:</b> A short sleep during the day<br><b>Example:</b> I'm going to take a cat nap before the meeting this afternoon.	
A Cat in Gloves Catches No Mice	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব সতর্ক থাকলে প্রয়োজনীয় জিনিস পাওয়া যায় না<br><b>English:</b> Being too cautious prevents you from getting what you need<br><b>Example:</b> You need to be more aggressive in negotiations - a cat in gloves catches no mice.	
A Cold Day In July	<b>Bengali:</b> যা কখনও ঘটবে না<br><b>English:</b> Something that will never happen<br><b>Example:</b> He'll apologize for his mistake when it's a cold day in July - meaning never.	
A Cold Fish	<b>Bengali:</b> যে ব্যক্তি আবেগ দ্বারা প্রভাবিত হয় না, কঠোর ও নিষ্ঠুর<br><b>English:</b> A person who is unemotional, harsh and cruel<br><b>Example:</b> The new manager is such a cold fish - he never shows any emotion or sympathy.	
A Cut Above	<b>Bengali:</b> সামান্য ভাল, উন্নত মানের<br><b>English:</b> Slightly better, of superior quality<br><b>Example:</b> This restaurant is a cut above the usual fast food places in the area.	
A Cut Below	<b>Bengali:</b> নিম্নমানের, কিছুটা খারাপ<br><b>English:</b> Of inferior quality, somewhat worse<br><b>Example:</b> The service at this hotel is a cut below what I expected for the price.	
A Day Late And A Dollar Short	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব দেরি এবং অপ্রতুল<br><b>English:</b> Too late and inadequate<br><b>Example:</b> His apology was a day late and a dollar short - the damage was already done.	
A Dog in The Manger	<b>Bengali:</b> যে স্বার্থপরভাবে অন্যদের  বাধা দেয়<br><b>English:</b> Someone who selfishly prevents others from using something<br><b>Example:</b> He's being a dog in the manger by not letting anyone else use the conference room.	
A Few Sandwiches Short Of A Picnic	<b>Bengali:</b> অস্বাভাবিকভাবে বোকা, পাগল<br><b>English:</b> Unusually stupid or crazy<br><b>Example:</b> I think our neighbor is a few sandwiches short of a picnic - he talks to his garden gnomes.	
A Good Deal	<b>Bengali:</b> অনেক পরিমাণে<br><b>English:</b> A large amount<br><b>Example:</b> She knows a good deal about ancient history from her university studies.	
A Guinea Pig	<b>Bengali:</b> পরীক্ষার জন্য ব্যবহৃত ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> A person used as a test subject<br><b>Example:</b> The company used early employees as guinea pigs for their new health insurance plan.	
A Hair's Breadth	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব ছোট দূরত্ব বা পরিমাণ<br><b>English:</b> A very small distance or amount<br><b>Example:</b> The bullet missed his heart by a hair's breadth - he was incredibly lucky.	
A Home Bird	<b>Bengali:</b> যে তার সামাজিক ও অবসর সময় ঘরে কাটাতে পছন্দ করে<br><b>English:</b> Someone who prefers to spend their social and leisure time at home<br><b>Example:</b> Unlike her party-loving sister, Mary is a home bird who enjoys quiet evenings.	
A Hundred And Ten Percent	<b>Bengali:</b> সর্বোচ্চের চেয়েও বেশি<br><b>English:</b> More than the maximum; complete effort<br><b>Example:</b> The team gave a hundred and ten percent in the championship game.	
A Lame Duck	<b>Bengali:</b> একজন ব্যক্তি বা প্রতিষ্ঠান যা সফল নয় এবং সাহায্যের প্রয়োজন<br><b>English:</b> A person or organization that is unsuccessful and needs help<br><b>Example:</b> The struggling airline became a lame duck that required government bailout.	
A Leg Up	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি সুবিধা, সহায়তা<br><b>English:</b> An advantage or assistance<br><b>Example:</b> Having a degree from Harvard gave him a leg up in the job market.	
A Lemon	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি যন্ত্র যা সঠিকভাবে কাজ করে না<br><b>English:</b> A defective or unsatisfactory product<br><b>Example:</b> The car I bought turned out to be a lemon - it broke down three times in the first month.	
A Life Of Its Own	<b>Bengali:</b> স্বাধীন অস্তিত্ব<br><b>English:</b> Independent existence<br><b>Example:</b> The rumor took on a life of its own and spread throughout the office.	
A Little Bird Told Me	<b>Bengali:</b> তথ্যের উৎস প্রকাশ করতে চাই না<br><b>English:</b> I don't want to reveal the source of information<br><b>Example:</b> A little bird told me you're getting promoted next week.	
A Little from Column A, a Little from Column B	<b>Bengali:</b> বিভিন্ন ধারণা থেকে কিছু নিয়ে একটি পদক্ষেপ<br><b>English:</b> Taking some elements from different ideas or approaches<br><b>Example:</b> Our solution was a little from column A, a little from column B - combining both strategies.	
A Lone Wolf	<b>Bengali:</b> যে অন্যদের সাথে খুব বেশি মেলামেশা করে না<br><b>English:</b> Someone who doesn't socialize much with others<br><b>Example:</b> Jake is a lone wolf who prefers working on projects by himself.	
A Lot on One's Plate	<b>Bengali:</b> অনেক কাজ থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Having many tasks or responsibilities<br><b>Example:</b> I can't take on another project right now - I have a lot on my plate.	
A Million and One	<b>Bengali:</b> অনেক, প্রচুর<br><b>English:</b> Very many, a large number<br><b>Example:</b> She has a million and one excuses for being late to work.	
A Notch Above	<b>Bengali:</b> উচ্চমানের, উন্নত<br><b>English:</b> Of higher quality, superior<br><b>Example:</b> This hotel is definitely a notch above the competition in terms of service.	
A Penny Saved is A Penny Earned	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রতিটি ছোট পরিমাণ সঞ্চয় গড়তে সাহায্য করে<br><b>English:</b> Every small amount saved helps build wealth<br><b>Example:</b> My grandmother always said 'a penny saved is a penny earned' when teaching us about money.	
A Penny for Your Thoughts	<b>Bengali:</b> তুমি কী ভাবছ?<br><b>English:</b> What are you thinking about?<br><b>Example:</b> You look so thoughtful staring out the window - a penny for your thoughts?	
A Picture Is Worth a Thousand Words	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি চিত্র হাজার শব্দের সমান<br><b>English:</b> An image can convey more than lengthy descriptions<br><b>Example:</b> Instead of explaining the damage, she just showed them the photo - a picture is worth a thousand words.	
A Plum Job	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি সহজ এবং আনন্দদায়ক কাজ যাতে ভাল বেতনও আছে<br><b>English:</b> An easy and enjoyable job with good pay<br><b>Example:</b> Working as a food critic for the magazine is really a plum job.	
A Rare Bird	<b>Bengali:</b> বিরল ব্যক্তি বা বস্তু<br><b>English:</b> A rare person or thing<br><b>Example:</b> An honest politician is truly a rare bird in today's world.	
A Scaredy-Cat	<b>Bengali:</b> যে অতিরিক্ত ভীত বা ভয় পায়<br><b>English:</b> Someone who is excessively afraid or fearful<br><b>Example:</b> Don't be such a scaredy-cat - it's just a harmless spider.	
A Second Bite At The Cherry	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু করার দ্বিতীয় সুযোগ<br><b>English:</b> A second chance to do something<br><b>Example:</b> After failing the exam, he was grateful to get a second bite at the cherry.	
A Sight for Sore Eyes	<b>Bengali:</b> এমন কেউ যাকে দেখে আনন্দিত হওয়া যায়<br><b>English:</b> Someone pleasant to see<br><b>Example:</b> After being away for months, seeing my family was a sight for sore eyes.	
A Sitting Duck	<b>Bengali:</b> দুর্বল অবস্থানে থাকা ব্যক্তি বা বস্তু<br><b>English:</b> A person or thing in a vulnerable position<br><b>Example:</b> Without security, the embassy was a sitting duck for terrorist attacks.	
A Snowball's Chance in Hell	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব কম বা কোন সম্ভাবনা নেই<br><b>English:</b> Very little or no possibility<br><b>Example:</b> He has a snowball's chance in hell of winning the lottery twice.	
A Stitch in Time Saves Nine	<b>Bengali:</b> দ্রুত সমস্যার সমাধান করলে পরে বড় সমস্যা এড়ানো যায়<br><b>English:</b> Solving problems quickly prevents bigger issues later<br><b>Example:</b> Fix that small leak now - a stitch in time saves nine.	
A Stone's Throw	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব কম দূরত্ব<br><b>English:</b> A very short distance<br><b>Example:</b> The library is just a stone's throw from my apartment.	
A Storm in a Teacup	<b>Bengali:</b> গুরুত্বহীন বিষয় নিয়ে অনর্থক রাগ বা চিন্তা<br><b>English:</b> Unnecessary anger or worry about unimportant matters<br><b>Example:</b> Their argument about the parking space was just a storm in a teacup.	
A Tall Order	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি কঠিন কাজ<br><b>English:</b> A difficult task<br><b>Example:</b> Finishing the project in one week is a tall order, but we'll try.	
A Week Is A Long Time In _____	<b>Bengali:</b> উল্লিখিত ক্ষেত্রে পরিস্থিতি দ্রুত পরিবর্তিত হতে পারে<br><b>English:</b> Situations can change rapidly in the mentioned field<br><b>Example:</b> A week is a long time in politics - public opinion can shift dramatically.	
About Time	<b>Bengali:</b> কাঙ্ক্ষিত সময়ের অনেক পরে<br><b>English:</b> Long overdue; finally happening<br><b>Example:</b> About time you showed up - we've been waiting for an hour!	
About To	<b>Bengali:</b> ঘটতে চলেছে, আসন্ন<br><b>English:</b> Going to happen soon, imminent<br><b>Example:</b> The movie is about to start, so we should find our seats.	
Above And Beyond	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রত্যাশিত বা প্রয়োজনীয়তার চেয়ে বেশি<br><b>English:</b> More than expected or required<br><b>Example:</b> The nurse went above and beyond to make the patient comfortable.	
Above Board	<b>Bengali:</b> খোলামেলা, প্রতারণা ছাড়া, সততার সাথে<br><b>English:</b> Open, honest, without deception<br><b>Example:</b> All our business dealings are completely above board.	
Above The Law	<b>Bengali:</b> আইনের উর্ধ্বে, আইনের বাইরে<br><b>English:</b> Not subject to legal restrictions<br><b>Example:</b> No one is above the law, not even the president.	
Above The Salt	<b>Bengali:</b> উচ্চ মর্যাদার বা সম্মানের<br><b>English:</b> Of high status or honor<br><b>Example:</b> In medieval times, sitting above the salt indicated noble status.	
Above Water	<b>Bengali:</b> চরম অসুবিধায় নেই, বিশেষত আর্থিকভাবে<br><b>English:</b> Not in extreme difficulty, especially financially<br><b>Example:</b> Despite the recession, the company managed to stay above water.	
Accident Of Birth	<b>Bengali:</b> পারিবারিক সৌভাগ্যের কারণে ভাগ্য<br><b>English:</b> Luck due to family circumstances<br><b>Example:</b> His wealth is merely an accident of birth - he inherited everything.	
Accident Waiting To Happen	<b>Bengali:</b> বিপজ্জনক পরিস্থিতি যা দুর্ঘটনার দিকে নিয়ে যেতে পারে<br><b>English:</b> A dangerous situation likely to cause an accident<br><b>Example:</b> That broken staircase is an accident waiting to happen.	
According To Hoyle	<b>Bengali:</b> যথাযথভাবে, স্থাপিত নিয়ম অনুসারে<br><b>English:</b> Properly, according to established rules<br><b>Example:</b> We played poker according to Hoyle - no variations or house rules.	
Ace In The Hole	<b>Bengali:</b> লুকানো সুবিধা<br><b>English:</b> A hidden advantage<br><b>Example:</b> His ace in the hole was his fluency in Mandarin Chinese.	
Ace Up One's Sleeve	<b>Bengali:</b> গোপন সুবিধা যা অন্যরা জানে না<br><b>English:</b> A secret advantage that others don't know about<br><b>Example:</b> She had an ace up her sleeve - a letter of recommendation from the CEO.	
Achilles' Heel	<b>Bengali:</b> অন্যথায় শক্তিশালী ব্যক্তি বা সংস্থার দুর্বল দিক<br><b>English:</b> The weak point of an otherwise strong person or organization<br><b>Example:</b> His temper is his Achilles' heel in business negotiations.	
Acid Test	<b>Bengali:</b> গুরুত্বপূর্ণ পরীক্ষা যা কিছুর মূল্য নির্ধারণ করে<br><b>English:</b> A crucial test that determines the value of something<br><b>Example:</b> The acid test of any relationship is how you handle disagreements.	
Acknowledge The Corn	<b>Bengali:</b> ভুল স্বীকার করা, নিজের ত্রুটি নির্দেশ করা<br><b>English:</b> To admit a mistake or acknowledge one's faults<br><b>Example:</b> After the evidence was presented, he had to acknowledge the corn.	
Acquired Taste	<b>Bengali:</b> বারবার চেষ্টার পর পছন্দ হওয়া বিষয়<br><b>English:</b> Something that becomes likeable after repeated exposure<br><b>Example:</b> Blue cheese is definitely an acquired taste - most people don't like it initially.	
Across The Board	<b>Bengali:</b> সব ক্ষেত্রে, সবার জন্য<br><b>English:</b> In all areas, for everyone<br><b>Example:</b> The company implemented salary increases across the board.	
Across The Pond	<b>Bengali:</b> আটলান্টিক মহাসাগরের অপর পারে<br><b>English:</b> On the other side of the Atlantic Ocean<br><b>Example:</b> My cousin lives across the pond in London.	
Act High and Mighty	<b>Bengali:</b> অহংকারী হওয়া, নিজেকে অন্যদের চেয়ে ভাল মনে করা<br><b>English:</b> To be arrogant, to think oneself better than others<br><b>Example:</b> Don't act high and mighty just because you got promoted.	
Act Of Congress	<b>Bengali:</b> কঠিন অনুমোদন পাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Something requiring difficult approval<br><b>Example:</b> Getting permission to renovate this historic building requires an act of Congress.	
Act One's Age	<b>Bengali:</b> পরিপক্ব হওয়া, শিশুসুলভ আচরণ না করা<br><b>English:</b> To behave maturely, not childishly<br><b>Example:</b> You're thirty years old - act your age and stop playing pranks.	
Actions Speak Louder Than Words	<b>Bengali:</b> কথার চেয়ে কাজ বেশি গুরুত্বপূর্ণ<br><b>English:</b> What you do is more important than what you say<br><b>Example:</b> He promised to help, but actions speak louder than words.	
Add Fuel To The Fire	<b>Bengali:</b> ইতিমধ্যে বিদ্যমান উত্তেজনা আরও বাড়ানো<br><b>English:</b> To make an existing conflict or tension worse<br><b>Example:</b> His sarcastic comment only added fuel to the fire during their argument.	
Add Insult To Injury	<b>Bengali:</b> পরাজয়ের সাথে অপমান যোগ করা<br><b>English:</b> To make a bad situation even worse<br><b>Example:</b> Not only did they fire him, but they also asked him to train his replacement - adding insult to injury.	
After One's Own Heart	<b>Bengali:</b> আনন্দদায়কভাবে অনুরূপ<br><b>English:</b> Pleasantly similar in character or interests<br><b>Example:</b> Meeting someone who loves hiking as much as I do - she's a woman after my own heart.	
After The Fact	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব দেরিতে, কিছু সম্পূর্ণ হওয়ার পর<br><b>English:</b> Too late, after something is completed<br><b>Example:</b> You can't change the contract after the fact - it's already signed.	
After The Lord Mayor's Show	<b>Bengali:</b> চিত্তাকর্ষক কিছুর পর নিরস লাগা<br><b>English:</b> Feeling anticlimactic after something impressive<br><b>Example:</b> After the spectacular opening ceremony, the regular events felt like after the Lord Mayor's show.	
Against The Clock	<b>Bengali:</b> সময়সীমা মেনে চলতে বাধ্য<br><b>English:</b> Under time pressure, racing against a deadline<br><b>Example:</b> We're working against the clock to finish this project by Friday.	
Against The Grain	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রাকৃতিক প্রবণতার বিপরীতে<br><b>English:</b> Contrary to natural tendency or normal practice<br><b>Example:</b> It goes against the grain for me to lie to my parents.	
Against The Run Of Play	<b>Bengali:</b> খেলার স্বাভাবিক গতির বিপরীতে<br><b>English:</b> Contrary to the normal flow of the game<br><b>Example:</b> Their goal came against the run of play - we had been dominating.	
Age Before Beauty	<b>Bengali:</b> বয়স্কদের আগে যাওয়ার সুযোগ দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Giving older people priority<br><b>Example:</b> After you, grandmother - age before beauty.	
Agree To Disagree	<b>Bengali:</b> মতবিরোধ মেনে নেওয়া বা পাশে রাখা<br><b>English:</b> To accept disagreement and move on<br><b>Example:</b> We'll never see eye to eye on politics, so let's agree to disagree.	
Agreement In Principle	<b>Bengali:</b> নীতিগতভাবে সম্মত হওয়া যেখানে সব বিস্তারিত ঠিক করা হয়নি<br><b>English:</b> General agreement where details haven't been worked out<br><b>Example:</b> We have an agreement in principle, but the lawyers need to finalize the terms.	
Aha Moment	<b>Bengali:</b> হঠাৎ অনুধাবন, হঠাৎ বুঝে ওঠা<br><b>English:</b> Sudden realization or understanding<br><b>Example:</b> I had an aha moment when I finally understood the math problem.	
Ahead Of One's Time	<b>Bengali:</b> সাধারণ প্রচলনের আগে ধারণা প্রদান, অত্যন্ত সৃজনশীল<br><b>English:</b> Having ideas before they become commonly accepted<br><b>Example:</b> Leonardo da Vinci was truly ahead of his time with his inventions.	
Ahead Of The Curve	<b>Bengali:</b> উদ্ভাবনী, অন্যদের আগে নতুন ধারণা প্রদান<br><b>English:</b> Innovative, ahead of others in new ideas<br><b>Example:</b> Apple has always been ahead of the curve in smartphone design.	
Ahead Of The Game	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রত্যাশিত গতির চেয়ে দ্রুত অগ্রগতি<br><b>English:</b> Making faster progress than expected<br><b>Example:</b> By finishing the report early, we're ahead of the game for once.	
Air Rage	<b>Bengali:</b> বিমানের ভিতরে রাগান্বিত আচরণ<br><b>English:</b> Angry behavior inside an aircraft<br><b>Example:</b> The passenger's air rage incident resulted in an emergency landing.	
Airy Fairy	<b>Bengali:</b> অযৌক্তিক, অবাস্তব<br><b>English:</b> Unrealistic or impractical<br><b>Example:</b> His business plan is too airy fairy - it lacks concrete details.	
Albatross Around One's Neck	<b>Bengali:</b> অতীতের কিছু যা বাধা হয়ে দাঁড়ায়<br><b>English:</b> Something from the past that becomes a burden<br><b>Example:</b> His criminal record is an albatross around his neck when job hunting.	
Alive and Kicking	<b>Bengali:</b> স্বাস্থ্য সমস্যা সত্ত্বেও ভাল স্বাস্থ্যে<br><b>English:</b> In good health despite health issues<br><b>Example:</b> Despite being ninety, my grandfather is still alive and kicking.	
All Along	<b>Bengali:</b> পুরো সময় জুড়ে<br><b>English:</b> Throughout the entire time<br><b>Example:</b> I knew all along that he was lying about his qualifications.	
All And Sundry	<b>Bengali:</b> সবাই (আলাদাভাবে)<br><b>English:</b> Everyone (individually)<br><b>Example:</b> She told all and sundry about her promotion at the office party.	
All Bark And No Bite	<b>Bengali:</b> হুমকি দেওয়ার প্রবণতা কিন্তু কার্যকর না করা<br><b>English:</b> Making threats but not following through<br><b>Example:</b> Don't worry about his angry words - he's all bark and no bite.	
All Dressed Up And Nowhere To Go	<b>Bengali:</b> কোনো অনুষ্ঠানের জন্য প্রস্তুত কিন্তু অনুষ্ঠান হলো না<br><b>English:</b> Ready for an event that gets cancelled<br><b>Example:</b> When the party was cancelled, I was all dressed up and nowhere to go.	
All Ears	<b>Bengali:</b> মনোযোগ সহকারে শোনা<br><b>English:</b> Listening attentively<br><b>Example:</b> Tell me about your vacation - I'm all ears.	
All Eyes And Ears	<b>Bengali:</b> মনোযোগী<br><b>English:</b> Very attentive<br><b>Example:</b> The children were all eyes and ears during the storytelling session.	
All Eyes Are On	<b>Bengali:</b> সবাই মনোযোগ দিচ্ছে<br><b>English:</b> Everyone is paying attention to<br><b>Example:</b> All eyes are on the new CEO to see how she'll handle the crisis.	
All Fur Coat And No Knickers	<b>Bengali:</b> বাহ্যিকভাবে আকর্ষণীয় কিন্তু গুণগত দিক থেকে খারাপ<br><b>English:</b> Attractive appearance but lacking substance<br><b>Example:</b> The fancy restaurant was all fur coat and no knickers - terrible food.	
All Hands on Deck	<b>Bengali:</b> সবাইকে সাহায্য করতে হবে<br><b>English:</b> Everyone needs to help<br><b>Example:</b> With the deadline approaching, it's all hands on deck to finish the project.	
All Hat And No Cattle	<b>Bengali:</b> দম্ভপূর্ণ, অভিমানী কিন্তু প্রকৃত গুণাবলী নেই<br><b>English:</b> Boastful but lacking real substance or ability<br><b>Example:</b> The new manager is all hat and no cattle - lots of talk but no results.	
All Hell Breaks Loose	<b>Bengali:</b> পরিস্থিতি বিশৃঙ্খল হয়ে ওঠে<br><b>English:</b> Chaos erupts<br><b>Example:</b> When the fire alarm went off during the meeting, all hell broke loose.	
All In A Day's Work	<b>Bengali:</b> এটা আমার দায়িত্বের মধ্যে<br><b>English:</b> Part of one's normal duties<br><b>Example:</b> Dealing with difficult customers is all in a day's work for a sales clerk.	
All In Good Time	"<b>Bengali:</b> অবশেষে, ভবিষ্যতে আরও অনুকূল সময়ে<br><b>English:</b> Eventually, at a more favorable time in the future<br><b>Example:</b> You'll get your promotion all in good time - just be patient.
All It's Cracked Up To Be"""	
Babe In The Woods	<b>Bengali:</b> নিষ্পাপ, সরল ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> An innocent, naive person<br><b>Example:</b> In the corporate world, he's just a babe in the woods.	
Babe Magnet	<b>Bengali:</b> যে পুরুষের প্রতি নারীরা আকৃষ্ট হয়<br><b>English:</b> A man who attracts women<br><b>Example:</b> With his charm and good looks, he's a real babe magnet.	
Baby Blues	<b>Bengali:</b> নীল চোখ<br><b>English:</b> Blue eyes<br><b>Example:</b> She has beautiful baby blues that sparkle when she smiles.	
Baby Boomer	<b>Bengali:</b> দ্বিতীয় বিশ্বযুদ্ধের পর জন্মগ্রহণকারী ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> Person born after World War II<br><b>Example:</b> My parents are baby boomers who lived through the 1960s.	
Babysitter Test	<b>Bengali:</b> গৃহস্থালীর যন্ত্রপাতি ব্যবহারের সহজতার মূল্যায়ন<br><b>English:</b> Evaluating how easy household appliances are to use<br><b>Example:</b> This remote control fails the babysitter test - it's too complicated.	
Back And Forth	<b>Bengali:</b> কথোপকথন, আলোচনা<br><b>English:</b> Conversation, discussion<br><b>Example:</b> The negotiations went back and forth for hours.	
Back At You	<b>Bengali:</b> তোমার জন্যও একই কথা<br><b>English:</b> The same to you<br><b>Example:</b> Happy birthday! - Back at you, it's your birthday too!	
Back Burner (On The)	<b>Bengali:</b> জরুরি নয়; পরের জন্য রেখে দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Not urgent; postponed<br><b>Example:</b> We'll put the renovation plans on the back burner for now.	
Back Forty	<b>Bengali:</b> দুর্গম, অগম্য ভূমি<br><b>English:</b> Remote, inaccessible land<br><b>Example:</b> He built his cabin in the back forty where no one could find him.	
Back Of Beyond	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি প্রত্যন্ত স্থান<br><b>English:</b> A very remote place<br><b>Example:</b> They live in the back of beyond, miles from civilization.	
Back Office	<b>Bengali:</b> ব্যবসার সহায়ক সেবা<br><b>English:</b> Support services of a business<br><b>Example:</b> While sales teams meet clients, back office staff handle paperwork.	
Back in the Day	<b>Bengali:</b> আগের দিনে, যখন আমি ছোট ছিলাম<br><b>English:</b> In the past, when I was younger<br><b>Example:</b> Back in the day, we didn't have smartphones.	
Back on One's Feet	<b>Bengali:</b> শারীরিকভাবে আবার সুস্থ হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Physically recovered again<br><b>Example:</b> After the surgery, it took months to get back on his feet.	
Back the Wrong Horse	<b>Bengali:</b> হারানো দলকে সমর্থন করা<br><b>English:</b> Support the losing side<br><b>Example:</b> I backed the wrong horse by investing in that failed startup.	
Back to Square One	<b>Bengali:</b> শুরুতে ফিরে যাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Return to the beginning<br><b>Example:</b> When the prototype failed, we were back to square one.	
Back to the Drawing Board	<b>Bengali:</b> আবার শুরু করতে বাধ্য হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Forced to start again<br><b>Example:</b> The design was rejected, so it's back to the drawing board.	
Back to the Salt Mines	<b>Bengali:</b> কাজে ফিরে যাওয়ার সময় হয়েছে<br><b>English:</b> Time to return to work<br><b>Example:</b> Lunch is over - back to the salt mines!	
Backing and Filling	<b>Bengali:</b> ছোটখাটো পরিবর্তন করে সিদ্ধান্ত বিলম্বিত করা<br><b>English:</b> Making minor changes while delaying decisions<br><b>Example:</b> The committee's backing and filling is frustrating everyone.	
Backseat Driver	<b>Bengali:</b> যে ব্যক্তি অনাকাঙ্ক্ষিত পরামর্শ দেয়<br><b>English:</b> Someone who gives unwanted advice<br><b>Example:</b> My mother-in-law is such a backseat driver about parenting.	
Bad Apple	<b>Bengali:</b> অসন্তুষ্ট, সমস্যা সৃষ্টিকারী বা অসৎ ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> A troublesome or dishonest person<br><b>Example:</b> One bad apple in the team can ruin the whole project.	
Bad Blood	<b>Bengali:</b> অতীতের কিছু থেকে উদ্ভূত শত্রুতা বা ঘৃণা<br><b>English:</b> Hostility or hatred arising from past events<br><b>Example:</b> There's bad blood between the two families from the old feud.	
Bad Egg	<b>Bengali:</b> যাকে বিশ্বাস করা যায় না<br><b>English:</b> Someone who cannot be trusted<br><b>Example:</b> Stay away from him - he's a bad egg who'll get you in trouble.	
Bad Taste In One's Mouth	<b>Bengali:</b> অস্বস্তি, কিছু ভুল আছে এমন অনুভূতি<br><b>English:</b> Discomfort, feeling that something is wrong<br><b>Example:</b> The way they fired him left a bad taste in my mouth.	
Bag of Tricks	<b>Bengali:</b> পদ্ধতি বা সম্পদের সংগ্রহ<br><b>English:</b> Collection of methods or resources<br><b>Example:</b> As a teacher, she has a whole bag of tricks to keep students engaged.	
Bail Out	<b>Bengali:</b> খারাপ পরিস্থিতি থেকে কাউকে উদ্ধার করা<br><b>English:</b> Rescue someone from a bad situation<br><b>Example:</b> The government had to bail out the failing banks.	
Ball and Chain	<b>Bengali:</b> স্ত্রী/স্বামী (নেতিবাচক কিন্তু প্রায়ই স্নেহপূর্ণ); চলমান বোঝা<br><b>English:</b> Spouse (negative but often affectionate); ongoing burden<br><b>Example:</b> He jokingly calls his wife his ball and chain.	
Ballpark Figure	<b>Bengali:</b> মোটামুটি অনুমান<br><b>English:</b> Rough estimate<br><b>Example:</b> Can you give me a ballpark figure for the renovation costs?	
Bang One's Head Against the Wall	<b>Bengali:</b> বারবার চেষ্টা করে কোনো অগ্রগতি না করা<br><b>English:</b> Repeatedly trying with no progress<br><b>Example:</b> I'm banging my head against the wall trying to solve this problem.	
Banner Year	<b>Bengali:</b> শক্তিশালী সাফল্যে চিহ্নিত বছর<br><b>English:</b> A year marked by strong success<br><b>Example:</b> 2023 was a banner year for the company's profits.	
Baptism by Fire	<b>Bengali:</b> নতুন দায়িত্ব নেওয়ার পরপরই কঠিন কাজ<br><b>English:</b> Difficult task immediately after taking new responsibility<br><b>Example:</b> His first day as manager was a baptism by fire with three crises.	
Bar Fly	<b>Bengali:</b> যে ব্যক্তি বারে অধিক সময় কাটায়<br><b>English:</b> A person who spends a lot of time in bars<br><b>Example:</b> The old bar fly knew everyone's story and all the local gossip.	
Bare One's Heart	<b>Bengali:</b> গভীর গোপন কথা স্বীকার করা<br><b>English:</b> Confess deep secrets<br><b>Example:</b> She bared her heart about her childhood fears to her therapist.	
Bark Up the Wrong Tree	<b>Bengali:</b> ভুল পদ্ধতি অনুসরণ করা<br><b>English:</b> Following the wrong approach<br><b>Example:</b> If you think I stole your lunch, you're barking up the wrong tree.	
Basket Case	<b>Bengali:</b> এতটাই বিপর্যস্ত যে কাজ করতে অক্ষম<br><b>English:</b> So distressed as to be unable to function<br><b>Example:</b> After the exam results, she was a complete basket case.	
Bat/Play for Both Teams	<b>Bengali:</b> উভকামী হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Being bisexual<br><b>Example:</b> He came out and said he plays for both teams.	
Batten Down the Hatches	<b>Bengali:</b> ঝড়ের জন্য প্রস্তুত হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Prepare for a storm<br><b>Example:</b> With the recession coming, it's time to batten down the hatches.	
Be A Barrel of Laughs	<b>Bengali:</b> মজাদার, হাস্যকর এবং আনন্দদায়ক হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Being fun, funny and entertaining<br><b>Example:</b> The comedy show was a barrel of laughs from start to finish.	
Be A Cold Day In Hell	<b>Bengali:</b> যা কখনো ঘটবে না<br><b>English:</b> Something that will never happen<br><b>Example:</b> It'll be a cold day in hell before he apologizes for his mistake.	
Be An Item	<b>Bengali:</b> দুজনের মধ্যে প্রেমের সম্পর্ক থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Two people being in a romantic relationship<br><b>Example:</b> Did you know that Sarah and Tom are an item now?	
Be Footloose and Fancy-Free	<b>Bengali:</b> দায়িত্বমুক্ত থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Being free from responsibilities<br><b>Example:</b> After retirement, he's footloose and fancy-free to travel anywhere.	
Be Head Over Heels	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো সাথে গভীর প্রেমে পড়া<br><b>English:</b> Being deeply in love with someone<br><b>Example:</b> She's head over heels in love with her new boyfriend.	
Be Like Chalk and Cheese	<b>Bengali:</b> সম্পূর্ণ আলাদা এবং অমিল<br><b>English:</b> Completely different and incompatible<br><b>Example:</b> The twins are like chalk and cheese - one loves sports, the other loves books.	
Be Lovey – Dovey	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রকাশ্যে ভালোবাসা প্রকাশ করা<br><b>English:</b> Publicly expressing affection<br><b>Example:</b> The newlyweds were so lovey-dovey at the party.	
Be Snowed Under	<b>Bengali:</b> কাজের চাপে অত্যন্ত ব্যস্ত থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Being extremely busy with work<br><b>Example:</b> I'm snowed under with assignments this week.	
Be in Seventh Heaven	<b>Bengali:</b> অত্যন্ত খুশি থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Being extremely happy<br><b>Example:</b> When she got the job offer, she was in seventh heaven.	
Be in Two Minds	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু নিয়ে নিশ্চিত না হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Being uncertain about something<br><b>Example:</b> I'm in two minds about whether to accept the job offer.	
Be on the Mend	<b>Bengali:</b> অসুস্থতার পর উন্নতি হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Improving after illness<br><b>Example:</b> After surgery, he's finally on the mend.	
Bean Counters	<b>Bengali:</b> হিসাবরক্ষক, আর্থিক পেশাদাররা<br><b>English:</b> Accountants, financial professionals<br><b>Example:</b> The bean counters said we need to cut costs by 20%.	
Beat Around the Bush	<b>Bengali:</b> অপ্রীতিকর বিষয় এড়িয়ে ঘুরিয়ে কথা বলা<br><b>English:</b> Avoiding unpleasant topics by speaking indirectly<br><b>Example:</b> Stop beating around the bush and tell me what happened.	
Beat Someone To The Draw	<b>Bengali:</b> অন্যের চেয়ে দ্রুত কিছু অর্জন করা<br><b>English:</b> Achieving something faster than others<br><b>Example:</b> He beat me to the draw and got the promotion first.	
Beat Someone to the Punch	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো আগে কিছু করা<br><b>English:</b> Do something before someone else<br><b>Example:</b> I was going to ask her out, but John beat me to the punch.	
Beat the Drum for	<b>Bengali:</b> সমর্থন আদায়ের জন্য কিছুর পক্ষে কথা বলা<br><b>English:</b> Speak in favor of something to gain support<br><b>Example:</b> The mayor is beating the drum for the new park proposal.	
Beauty Is Only Skin Deep	<b>Bengali:</b> বাহ্যিক সৌন্দর্য একটি ভাসা ভাসা ভিত্তি<br><b>English:</b> External beauty is a superficial basis<br><b>Example:</b> Don't judge people by looks - beauty is only skin deep.	
Bed of Roses	<b>Bengali:</b> আরামদায়ক পরিস্থিতি<br><b>English:</b> A comfortable situation<br><b>Example:</b> Marriage isn't always a bed of roses - it requires work.	
Bedroom Eyes	<b>Bengali:</b> যৌনতার আমন্ত্রণ জানানো চোখের ভাব<br><b>English:</b> Seductive eye expression<br><b>Example:</b> The actress was famous for her bedroom eyes in romantic scenes.	
Bee in One's Bonnet	<b>Bengali:</b> কোনো ধারণা মাথায় ঢুকে থাকা<br><b>English:</b> An idea stuck in one's head<br><b>Example:</b> He has a bee in his bonnet about organic farming.	
Beggar Thy Neighbor	<b>Bengali:</b> অন্যদের ক্ষতির কথা না ভেবে নিজের জন্য কিছু করা<br><b>English:</b> Doing something for oneself without considering harm to others<br><b>Example:</b> The tariff policy was a beggar thy neighbor approach to trade.	
Behind the Eight Ball	<b>Bengali:</b> গুরুতর অসুবিধায় পড়া<br><b>English:</b> In serious difficulty<br><b>Example:</b> With mounting debts, the company is behind the eight ball.	
Behind the Scenes	<b>Bengali:</b> জনসাধারণের কাছে প্রকাশ্য নয় এমনভাবে<br><b>English:</b> In a way not visible to the public<br><b>Example:</b> She works behind the scenes to organize the charity events.	
Behind the Times	<b>Bengali:</b> পুরনো ধাঁচের<br><b>English:</b> Old-fashioned<br><b>Example:</b> My grandfather is behind the times when it comes to technology.	
Bell the Cat	<b>Bengali:</b> কঠিন বা অসম্ভব কাজ নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Taking on a difficult or impossible task<br><b>Example:</b> Someone needs to bell the cat and tell the boss about the problem.	
Bells And Whistles	<b>Bengali:</b> পণ্যের আকর্ষণীয় কিন্তু অপ্রয়োজনীয় বৈশিষ্ট্য<br><b>English:</b> Attractive but unnecessary features of a product<br><b>Example:</b> This car has all the bells and whistles but costs too much.	
Belly Laugh	<b>Bengali:</b> জোরে, হৃদয় থেকে হাসি<br><b>English:</b> Loud, hearty laughter<br><b>Example:</b> His joke got a real belly laugh from the audience.	
Bend an Elbow	<b>Bengali:</b> পানশালায় মদ পান করা<br><b>English:</b> Drinking alcohol at a bar<br><b>Example:</b> After work, they went to bend an elbow at the local pub.	
Best Thing Since Sliced Bread	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি উদ্ভাবনী উন্নতি<br><b>English:</b> An innovative improvement<br><b>Example:</b> This new smartphone is the best thing since sliced bread.	
Best of Both Worlds	<b>Bengali:</b> সাধারণত পৃথক দুটি গুণের সমন্বয়<br><b>English:</b> Combination of two usually separate advantages<br><b>Example:</b> Working from home gives me the best of both worlds - career and family time.	
Bet One's Bottom Dollar	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু ঘটবে বলে নিশ্চিত থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Being certain something will happen<br><b>Example:</b> You can bet your bottom dollar he'll be late again.	
Bet the Farm	<b>Bengali:</b> সবকিছু ঝুঁকিতে ফেলা<br><b>English:</b> Risk everything<br><b>Example:</b> He bet the farm on that startup and lost everything.	
Better Late Than Never	<b>Bengali:</b> দেরিতে হলেও না করার চেয়ে ভালো<br><b>English:</b> Even if late, it's better than not doing it<br><b>Example:</b> You finally called - better late than never!	
Between a Rock and a Hard Place	<b>Bengali:</b> দুটি অবাঞ্ছিত বিকল্পের মাঝে আটকে পড়া<br><b>English:</b> Stuck between two undesirable alternatives<br><b>Example:</b> I'm between a rock and a hard place - stay in a bad job or be unemployed.	
Between the Devil and the Deep Blue Sea	<b>Bengali:</b> কঠিন অবস্থানে থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Being in a difficult position<br><b>Example:</b> With bills due and no job, he's between the devil and the deep blue sea.	
Beyond the Pale	<b>Bengali:</b> নৈতিক বা সামাজিকভাবে চরম<br><b>English:</b> Morally or socially extreme<br><b>Example:</b> His behavior at the meeting was beyond the pale.	
Beyond the Shadow of a Doubt	<b>Bengali:</b> একেবারে নিশ্চিত<br><b>English:</b> Absolutely certain<br><b>Example:</b> He's guilty beyond the shadow of a doubt.	
Big Apple	<b>Bengali:</b> নিউ ইয়র্ক শহরের অনানুষ্ঠানিক নাম<br><b>English:</b> Informal name for New York City<br><b>Example:</b> She moved to the Big Apple to pursue her acting career.	
Big Brother	<b>Bengali:</b> নাগরিকদের জীবনে অনুপ্রবেশকারী সরকার<br><b>English:</b> Government that intrudes into citizens' lives<br><b>Example:</b> Privacy advocates worry about Big Brother watching our online activities.	
Big Cheese	<b>Bengali:</b> কোম্পানি বা সংস্থার গুরুত্বপূর্ণ ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> Important person in a company or organization<br><b>Example:</b> The big cheese is coming to visit our branch next week.	
Big Deal	<b>Bengali:</b> গুরুত্বপূর্ণ ঘটনা বা অর্জন<br><b>English:</b> Important event or achievement<br><b>Example:</b> Getting into Harvard is a really big deal for our family.	
Big Fish	<b>Bengali:</b> গুরুত্বপূর্ণ ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> Important person<br><b>Example:</b> In this small town, the mayor is the big fish.	
Big Picture	<b>Bengali:</b> বিস্তৃত দৃষ্টিভঙ্গি<br><b>English:</b> Broad perspective<br><b>Example:</b> Don't get lost in details - focus on the big picture.	
Big Time	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব বেশি মাত্রায়<br><b>English:</b> To a great extent<br><b>Example:</b> He messed up big time with that presentation.	
Birds of a Feather	<b>Bengali:</b> একই ধরনের চরিত্র বা আগ্রহের মানুষ<br><b>English:</b> People with similar character or interests<br><b>Example:</b> John and Mike are birds of a feather - both love fishing.	
Bite Off More Than You Can Chew	<b>Bengali:</b> সক্ষমতার চেয়ে বেশি করার চেষ্টা করা<br><b>English:</b> Attempting more than one's capability<br><b>Example:</b> Taking five courses this semester - I bit off more than I can chew.	
Bite the Bullet	<b>Bengali:</b> যন্ত্রণা সত্ত্বেও কিছু করা<br><b>English:</b> Do something despite pain or difficulty<br><b>Example:</b> I need to bite the bullet and tell him the truth.	
Bite the Hand That Feeds You	<b>Bengali:</b> যে সাহায্য করেছে তার সাথে খারাপ ব্যবহার করা<br><b>English:</b> Treat badly someone who has helped you<br><b>Example:</b> Criticizing your boss is biting the hand that feeds you.	
Bitter Pill to Swallow	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি অপ্রীতিকর সত্য যা মেনে নিতে হবে<br><b>English:</b> An unpleasant truth that must be accepted<br><b>Example:</b> Losing the championship was a bitter pill to swallow.	
Black Eye	<b>Bengali:</b> লজ্জার দাগ<br><b>English:</b> A mark of shame<br><b>Example:</b> The scandal gave the company a black eye in the media.	
Black Sheep	<b>Bengali:</b> দলে খাপ খায় না এমন ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> A person who doesn't fit in with the group<br><b>Example:</b> He's the black sheep of the family - everyone else is a doctor.	
Black and White	<b>Bengali:</b> ভালো-মন্দের স্পষ্ট পার্থক্য<br><b>English:</b> Clear distinction between good and bad<br><b>Example:</b> The issue isn't black and white - there are many gray areas.	
Black-and-Blue	<b>Bengali:</b> আঘাতপ্রাপ্ত, ক্ষতচিহ্ন<br><b>English:</b> Bruised, with marks from injury<br><b>Example:</b> After the fall, his arm was black-and-blue.	
Blank Check	<b>Bengali:</b> যা ইচ্ছা খরচ বা করার অনুমতি<br><b>English:</b> Permission to spend or do whatever one wants<br><b>Example:</b> The CEO gave him a blank check to fix the department.	
Blind Date	<b>Bengali:</b> অচেনা দুজনের মধ্যে ডেট<br><b>English:</b> A date between two strangers<br><b>Example:</b> My friend set me up on a blind date with her colleague.	
Blinded by Love	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রেমে অন্ধ হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Unable to see faults because of love<br><b>Example:</b> She's blinded by love and can't see his obvious flaws.	
Blood and Thunder	<b>Bengali:</b> নাটকীয়, চমৎকার পারফরমেন্স<br><b>English:</b> Dramatic, spectacular performance<br><b>Example:</b> The politician's blood and thunder speech rallied the crowd.	
Blow Away the Cobwebs	<b>Bengali:</b> আরো প্রাণবন্ত করা, নতুন ধারণা সৃষ্টি করা<br><b>English:</b> Make more lively, create fresh ideas<br><b>Example:</b> A walk in the park will blow away the cobwebs after studying all day.	
Blow Hot and Cold	<b>Bengali:</b> উৎসাহের মাত্রা বারবার পরিবর্তন করা<br><b>English:</b> Repeatedly changing levels of enthusiasm<br><b>Example:</b> He blows hot and cold about the project - one day excited, next day pessimistic.	
Blow Off Steam	<b>Bengali:</b> ক্রোধ ও হতাশা প্রকাশ করা<br><b>English:</b> Express anger and frustration<br><b>Example:</b> He went to the gym to blow off steam after the stressful meeting.	
Blow One's Stack	<b>Bengali:</b> রাগে ফেটে পড়া<br><b>English:</b> Explode in anger<br><b>Example:</b> When he saw the mess, he really blew his stack.	
Blow One's Top	<b>Bengali:</b> রাগ হারানো<br><b>English:</b> Lose one's temper<br><b>Example:</b> She blew her top when she found out about the lie.	
Blow Up	<b>Bengali:</b> বিস্ফোরিত হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Explode or become very angry<br><b>Example:</b> The argument blew up into a major fight.	
Blow Your Own Trumpet	<b>Bengali:</b> আত্মপ্রশংসা করা<br><b>English:</b> Praise oneself<br><b>Example:</b> Don't blow your own trumpet - let your work speak for itself.	
Blow the Cobwebs Away	<b>Bengali:</b> নতুন ধারণার জন্য জায়গা করা<br><b>English:</b> Make room for fresh ideas<br><b>Example:</b> The new manager will blow the cobwebs away with innovative strategies.	
Blow the Whistle	<b>Bengali:</b> কর্তৃপক্ষের কাছে অবৈধ কার্যকলাপ জানানো<br><b>English:</b> Report illegal activities to authorities<br><b>Example:</b> The employee blew the whistle on the company's tax evasion.	
Blue Blood	<b>Bengali:</b> অভিজাত পটভূমির ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> Person from aristocratic background<br><b>Example:</b> She comes from blue blood - her family has been nobility for centuries.	
Blue Eyed Boy	<b>Bengali:</b> কর্তৃপক্ষের প্রিয় ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> Person favored by authority<br><b>Example:</b> He's the boss's blue eyed boy and gets all the best assignments.	
Blue Light Special	<b>Bengali:</b> ছাড়ের দোকানে অস্থায়ী বিক্রয়<br><b>English:</b> Temporary sale at a discount store<br><b>Example:</b> I got this sweater on a blue light special at the department store.	
Bob's Your Uncle	<b>Bengali:</b> বাকিটা সহজ; প্রায় শেষ<br><b>English:</b> The rest is easy; almost finished<br><b>Example:</b> Just add water, mix it up, and Bob's your uncle - perfect cake batter!	
Bolt From the Blue	<b>Bengali:</b> সম্পূর্ণ অপ্রত্যাশিত কিছু<br><b>English:</b> Something completely unexpected<br><b>Example:</b> His resignation was a bolt from the blue - nobody saw it coming.	
Bone Dry	<b>Bengali:</b> সম্পূর্ণ শুকনো<br><b>English:</b> Completely dry<br><b>Example:</b> After the drought, the riverbed was bone dry.	
Born on The Wrong Side of the Blanket	<b>Bengali:</b> অবিবাহিত বাবা-মায়ের সন্তান<br><b>English:</b> Child of unmarried parents<br><b>Example:</b> In those days, being born on the wrong side of the blanket carried social stigma.	
Borrow Trouble	<b>Bengali:</b> অপ্রয়োজনীয় ঝুঁকি নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Take unnecessary risks<br><b>Example:</b> Don't borrow trouble by confronting him when he's angry.	
Bottom of the Barrel	<b>Bengali:</b> নিম্নমানের পছন্দ<br><b>English:</b> Lowest quality choice<br><b>Example:</b> These are bottom of the barrel candidates - we need better options.	
Boy Toy	<b>Bengali:</b> বয়স্ক নারীর তরুণ প্রেমিক<br><b>English:</b> Young lover of an older woman<br><b>Example:</b> The wealthy widow's boy toy was half her age.	
Boys will be Boys	<b>Bengali:</b> ছেলেরা যখন সমস্যায় পড়ে তখন বলা কথা<br><b>English:</b> Said when boys get into trouble<br><b>Example:</b> When they broke the window playing ball, she just said 'boys will be boys.'	
Brainstorm	<b>Bengali:</b> দ্রুত অনেক ধারণা তৈরি করা<br><b>English:</b> Generate many ideas quickly<br><b>Example:</b> Let's brainstorm solutions to this marketing problem.	
Break Out in A Cold Sweat	<b>Bengali:</b> জ্বর বা উদ্বেগে ঘেমে যাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Sweat from fever or anxiety<br><b>Example:</b> I broke out in a cold sweat when I realized I'd forgotten the presentation.	
Break The Ice	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু শুরু করা, বিশেষত সামাজিক পরিচয়ের মাধ্যমে<br><b>English:</b> Start something, especially social interaction<br><b>Example:</b> He told a joke to break the ice at the awkward dinner party.	
Break a Leg	<b>Bengali:</b> শুভকামনা!<br><b>English:</b> Good luck! (especially in theater)<br><b>Example:</b> Break a leg in your audition tonight!	
Break the Bank	<b>Bengali:</b> আর্থিক সম্পদ নিঃশেষ করা<br><b>English:</b> Exhaust financial resources<br><b>Example:</b> This vacation will break the bank, but it's worth it.	
Break up/Split up	<b>Bengali:</b> সম্পর্ক শেষ করা<br><b>English:</b> End a relationship<br><b>Example:</b> They broke up after dating for three years.	
Bring Home the Bacon	<b>Bengali:</b> পরিবারের জন্য অর্থ উপার্জন করা<br><b>English:</b> Earn money for the family<br><b>Example:</b> As the sole breadwinner, she brings home the bacon for her family.	
Bringing a Knife to a Gunfight	<b>Bengali:</b> অপ্রস্তুত বা অযোগ্য সরঞ্জাম নিয়ে আসা<br><b>English:</b> Coming unprepared or with inadequate equipment<br><b>Example:</b> Trying to compete with that small budget is like bringing a knife to a gunfight.	
Brush Under the Carpet	<b>Bengali:</b> সমস্যা বা ভুল সাময়িকভাবে লুকানো<br><b>English:</b> Temporarily hide problems or mistakes<br><b>Example:</b> Don't brush this issue under the carpet - we need to address it.	
Bucket List	<b>Bengali:</b> মৃত্যুর আগে যা দেখতে বা করতে চান<br><b>English:</b> Things you want to see or do before you die<br><b>Example:</b> Visiting the Grand Canyon is on my bucket list.	
Bull in a China Shop	<b>Bengali:</b> আনাড়ি বা কূটনীতিহীন ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> Clumsy or undiplomatic person<br><b>Example:</b> He's like a bull in a china shop at formal events.	
Bump in the Road	<b>Bengali:</b> অস্থায়ী সমস্যা, ছোট বিপত্তি<br><b>English:</b> Temporary problem, minor setback<br><b>Example:</b> This delay is just a bump in the road - we'll still finish on time.	
Bundle Up	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রচুর গরম কাপড় পরা<br><b>English:</b> Wear lots of warm clothes<br><b>Example:</b> Bundle up before going outside - it's freezing!	
Burn One's Bridges	<b>Bengali:</b> চাকরি বা সম্পর্ক এত খারাপভাবে শেষ করা যে যোগাযোগ থাকে না<br><b>English:</b> End job or relationship so badly that contact is impossible<br><b>Example:</b> Don't burn your bridges when you quit - you might need a reference.	
Burn the Candle at Both Ends	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব বেশি সময় কাজ করা<br><b>English:</b> Work too many hours<br><b>Example:</b> Working two jobs means burning the candle at both ends.	
Burn the Midnight Oil	<b>Bengali:</b> রাত গভীর পর্যন্ত কাজ করা<br><b>English:</b> Work late into the night<br><b>Example:</b> I'll have to burn the midnight oil to finish this report.	
Bury One's Head In the Sand	<b>Bengali:</b> সুস্পষ্ট ভুল উপেক্ষা করা, বাস্তবতার মুখোমুখি না হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Ignore obvious problems, not face reality<br><b>Example:</b> Stop burying your head in the sand - we need to address these issues.	
Bury the Hatchet	<b>Bengali:</b> শান্তি স্থাপন করা, বিবাদ শেষ করতে সম্মত হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Make peace, agree to end disputes<br><b>Example:</b> After years of fighting, the brothers finally buried the hatchet.	
Business as Usual	<b>Bengali:</b> স্বাভাবিক অবস্থা<br><b>English:</b> Normal conditions<br><b>Example:</b> Despite the renovation, it's business as usual at the office.	
Busman's Holiday	<b>Bengali:</b> কাজের মতো ছুটি কাটানো<br><b>English:</b> Spending vacation doing work-like activities<br><b>Example:</b> The chef's busman's holiday was cooking for his family reunion.	
Busted Flush	<b>Bengali:</b> ব্যর্থতা, আশাব্যঞ্জক কিন্তু অসফল কিছু<br><b>English:</b> Failure, something promising but unsuccessful<br><b>Example:</b> His business venture turned out to be a busted flush.	
Butter Wouldn't Melt in Someone's Mouth	<b>Bengali:</b> ব্যবহারে শান্ত, ভদ্র এবং নিয়মানুবর্তী<br><b>English:</b> Appearing calm, polite and well-behaved<br><b>Example:</b> She looks like butter wouldn't melt in her mouth, but she's quite mischievous.	
Buy Time	<b>Bengali:</b> অবস্থানের উন্নতির লক্ষ্যে বিলম্ব ঘটানো<br><b>English:</b> Delay to improve one's position<br><b>Example:</b> We need to buy time while we develop a better strategy.	
Buy a Pig in a Poke	<b>Bengali:</b> পূর্ব পরীক্ষা ছাড়াই কিছু কেনা<br><b>English:</b> Buy something without prior examination<br><b>Example:</b> Buying that used car online was like buying a pig in a poke.	
By All Means	<b>Bengali:</b> অবশ্যই, নিশ্চিতভাবে<br><b>English:</b> Certainly, definitely<br><b>Example:</b> By all means, take as much time as you need.	
By Hook or by Crook	<b>Bengali:</b> সম্ভবত অসৎ উপায়ে<br><b>English:</b> By possibly dishonest means<br><b>Example:</b> He'll get that promotion by hook or by crook.	
By Word of Mouth	<b>Bengali:</b> লিখিত মাধ্যমের পরিবর্তে ব্যক্তিগত যোগাযোগের মাধ্যমে<br><b>English:</b> Through personal communication rather than written means<br><b>Example:</b> The news spread by word of mouth throughout the neighborhood.	
By a Whisker	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব কম ব্যবধানে<br><b>English:</b> By a very small margin<br><b>Example:</b> She won the race by a whisker - just 0.01 seconds ahead.	
By the Skin of One's Teeth	<b>Bengali:</b> সবেমাত্র দুর্যোগ এড়ানো<br><b>English:</b> Just barely avoiding disaster<br><b>Example:</b> He passed the exam by the skin of his teeth with a score of 51%.	
Call It a Day	<b>Bengali:</b> দিনের কাজ শেষ করা<br><b>English:</b> End the day's work<br><b>Example:</b> It's 6 PM - let's call it a day and go home.	
Call It a Night	<b>Bengali:</b> রাতের কাজ শেষ করে ঘরে যাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> End night activities and go home<br><b>Example:</b> After three movies, they decided to call it a night.	
Call the Shots	<b>Bengali:</b> গুরুত্বপূর্ণ সিদ্ধান্ত নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Make important decisions<br><b>Example:</b> As the CEO, she calls the shots in the company.	
Call the Tune	<b>Bengali:</b> গুরুত্বপূর্ণ সিদ্ধান্ত নিয়ে পরিস্থিতি নিয়ন্ত্রণ করা<br><b>English:</b> Control the situation by making key decisions<br><b>Example:</b> The investors call the tune in this startup.	
Can't See the Forest for the Trees	<b>Bengali:</b> বিস্তৃত দৃষ্টিভঙ্গি রাখতে পারা না<br><b>English:</b> Unable to maintain a broad perspective<br><b>Example:</b> You're so focused on minor details, you can't see the forest for the trees.	
Can't Swing A Dead Cat Without Hitting	<b>Bengali:</b> অনেক উদাহরণ পাওয়া যায়<br><b>English:</b> Many examples can be found<br><b>Example:</b> You can't swing a dead cat without hitting a coffee shop in this neighborhood.	
Carrot-and-Stick Approach	<b>Bengali:</b> পুরস্কার ও শাস্তির পদ্ধতি<br><b>English:</b> Method of rewards and punishments<br><b>Example:</b> The manager uses a carrot-and-stick approach to motivate employees.	
Carry a Torch for	<b>Bengali:</b> সম্পর্ক শেষ হওয়ার পরেও ভালোবাসা অব্যাহত রাখা<br><b>English:</b> Continue loving someone after relationship ends<br><b>Example:</b> He's been carrying a torch for his ex-girlfriend for years.	
Carry Coals To Newcastle	<b>Bengali:</b> অপ্রয়োজনীয় কিছু সরবরাহ করা<br><b>English:</b> Supply something unnecessary<br><b>Example:</b> Bringing pizza to an Italian restaurant is like carrying coals to Newcastle.	
Carry the Can	<b>Bengali:</b> অন্যের দোষের দায় নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Take responsibility for others' mistakes<br><b>Example:</b> The assistant had to carry the can for his boss's error.	
Cash In One's Chips	<b>Bengali:</b> দ্রুত লাভ নেওয়া বা মৃত্যুবরণ করা<br><b>English:</b> Take quick profit or die<br><b>Example:</b> After winning big at poker, he decided to cash in his chips.	
Cash-Strapped	<b>Bengali:</b> টাকার অভাবে পড়া<br><b>English:</b> Lacking money<br><b>Example:</b> The cash-strapped company had to lay off employees.	
Cast the First Stone	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রথম সমালোচনা বা আক্রমণ করা<br><b>English:</b> Make the first criticism or attack<br><b>Example:</b> Those without sin should cast the first stone.	
Castle in the Air	<b>Bengali:</b> অবাস্তব পরিকল্পনা<br><b>English:</b> Unrealistic plans<br><b>Example:</b> His business plan is just a castle in the air with no foundation.	
Cat Fight	<b>Bengali:</b> দুই নারীর মধ্যে লড়াই<br><b>English:</b> Fight between two women<br><b>Example:</b> The argument turned into a cat fight over the promotion.	
Cat Got Your Tongue	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু বলার নেই?<br><b>English:</b> Nothing to say?<br><b>Example:</b> You're unusually quiet - cat got your tongue?	
Cat on a hot tin roof	<b>Bengali:</b> অত্যন্ত নার্ভাস হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Being extremely nervous<br><b>Example:</b> Waiting for the test results, he was like a cat on a hot tin roof.	
Cat-and-Mouse	<b>Bengali:</b> খেলাচ্ছলে অপ্রীতিকর আচরণ<br><b>English:</b> Playfully unpleasant behavior<br><b>Example:</b> The detective played cat-and-mouse with the suspect during questioning.	
Cat's Paw	<b>Bengali:</b> অন্যের হাতিয়ার হিসেবে ব্যবহৃত ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> Person used as a tool by others<br><b>Example:</b> He was just a cat's paw in their scheme to embezzle money.	
Catch One's Death of Cold	<b>Bengali:</b> গুরুতর ঠাণ্ডা লাগা<br><b>English:</b> Catch a severe cold<br><b>Example:</b> Bundle up or you'll catch your death of cold in this weather!	
Catch Some Rays	<b>Bengali:</b> রোদে বসা বা শোয়া<br><b>English:</b> Sit or lie in the sun<br><b>Example:</b> Let's go to the beach and catch some rays this weekend.	
Catch Someone's Eye	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো দৃষ্টি আকর্ষণ করা<br><b>English:</b> Attract someone's attention<br><b>Example:</b> The red dress in the window caught her eye.	
Catch-22	<b>Meaning:</b> A paradoxical situation from which an individual cannot escape because of contradictory rules. <br><br> <b>Origin:</b> From Joseph Heller’s 1961 novel; a pilot can be grounded if he's crazy, but asking to be grounded proves he's sane. <br><br> <b>Example:</b> I can't get a job without experience, but I can't get experience without a job—it's a Catch-22.	
Caught Red-Handed	<b>Bengali:</b> অপরাধের সময় ধরা পড়া<br><b>English:</b> Caught in the act of committing a crime<br><b>Example:</b> The thief was caught red-handed stealing from the cash register.	
Champagne taste on a beer budget	<b>Bengali:</b> আর্থিক সামর্থ্যের চেয়ে বেশি খরচের পছন্দ<br><b>English:</b> Having expensive preferences beyond one's financial means<br><b>Example:</b> She has champagne taste on a beer budget - always wanting luxury items.	
Change Horses in Midstream	<b>Bengali:</b> মাঝপথে পরিকল্পনা বা নেতৃত্ব বদলানো<br><b>English:</b> Change plans or leadership midway<br><b>Example:</b> It's risky to change horses in midstream during this critical project.	
Change of Heart	<b>Bengali:</b> মতামত বা দৃষ্টিভঙ্গি পরিবর্তন<br><b>English:</b> Change of opinion or perspective<br><b>Example:</b> She had a change of heart and decided to accept the job offer.	
Change One's Tune	<b>Bengali:</b> কোনো বিষয়ে মতামত পরিবর্তন করা<br><b>English:</b> Change one's opinion about something<br><b>Example:</b> He changed his tune about remote work after trying it himself.	
Changing of the Guard	<b>Bengali:</b> নেতৃত্ব পরিবর্তন<br><b>English:</b> Change in leadership<br><b>Example:</b> The company is experiencing a changing of the guard with the new CEO.	
Chase Rainbows	<b>Bengali:</b> অবাস্তব লক্ষ্য অনুসরণ করা<br><b>English:</b> Pursue unrealistic goals<br><b>Example:</b> Stop chasing rainbows and focus on achievable objectives.	
Cheap Shot	<b>Bengali:</b> অন্যায় আক্রমণ<br><b>English:</b> Unfair attack<br><b>Example:</b> Bringing up his past mistakes was a cheap shot during the debate.	
Cherry-Pick	<b>Bengali:</b> নিজের সুবিধামতো প্রমাণ উপস্থাপন করা<br><b>English:</b> Present evidence selectively for one's advantage<br><b>Example:</b> Don't cherry-pick data to support your argument - show the complete picture.	
Chew the Fat	<b>Bengali:</b> দীর্ঘ সময় গল্প করা<br><b>English:</b> Chat for a long time<br><b>Example:</b> The old friends spent hours chewing the fat about their school days.	
Chickens Come Home To Roost	<b>Bengali:</b> পূর্বকর্মের নেতিবাচক ফল পাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Face negative consequences of past actions<br><b>Example:</b> His dishonesty finally caught up with him - the chickens came home to roost.	
Child's Play	<b>Bengali:</b> অত্যন্ত সহজ কাজ<br><b>English:</b> Extremely easy task<br><b>Example:</b> For a computer expert, fixing this issue is child's play.	
Chill Out	<b>Bengali:</b> শান্ত হওয়া এবং বিশ্রাম নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Relax and calm down<br><b>Example:</b> Chill out - there's no need to get so stressed about the exam.	
Chin Music	<b>Bengali:</b> অর্থহীন কথাবার্তা<br><b>English:</b> Meaningless talk<br><b>Example:</b> Stop the chin music and get to the point.	
Chin Up	<b>Bengali:</b> সাহস রাখা<br><b>English:</b> Keep courage<br><b>Example:</b> Chin up! Things will get better soon.	
Chip off the Old Block	<b>Bengali:</b> পিতার মতো সন্তান<br><b>English:</b> Child who resembles the parent<br><b>Example:</b> He's a chip off the old block - just as stubborn as his father.	
Chomp at the Bit	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু করার জন্য আগ্রহী হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Being eager to do something<br><b>Example:</b> The athletes were chomping at the bit to start the race.	
Chop Chop	<b>Bengali:</b> দ্রুত, তাড়াতাড়ি<br><b>English:</b> Quickly, hurry up<br><b>Example:</b> Chop chop! We need to leave in five minutes.	
Chop Shop	<b>Bengali:</b> চুরি করা গাড়ির যন্ত্রাংশ বিক্রির দোকান<br><b>English:</b> Shop selling parts from stolen cars<br><b>Example:</b> The police raided the chop shop and arrested the criminals.	
Chuck a Wobbly	<b>Bengali:</b> আবেগপ্রবণ আচরণ করা<br><b>English:</b> Have an emotional outburst<br><b>Example:</b> She chucked a wobbly when she heard the bad news.	
Circle the Wagons	<b>Bengali:</b> আক্রমণের বিরুদ্ধে প্রতিরক্ষামূলক অবস্থান নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Take defensive position against attack<br><b>Example:</b> When the scandal broke, the company circled the wagons.	
Claim to Fame	<b>Bengali:</b> অস্বাভাবিক বৈশিষ্ট্য বা অফার<br><b>English:</b> Unusual feature or achievement<br><b>Example:</b> The town's claim to fame is having the world's largest ball of yarn.	
Clean Up Nicely	<b>Bengali:</b> সাজগোজ করলে সুন্দর দেখানো<br><b>English:</b> Look good when dressed up<br><b>Example:</b> He may look scruffy normally, but he cleans up nicely for formal events.	
Clear the Air	<b>Bengali:</b> উত্তেজনা কমানো, সৎ আলোচনার মাধ্যমে দ্বন্দ্ব নিরসন<br><b>English:</b> Reduce tension, resolve conflict through honest discussion<br><b>Example:</b> We need to have a meeting to clear the air about these misunderstandings.	
Clip Someone's Wings	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো সুবিধা বা স্বাধীনতা কমানো<br><b>English:</b> Reduce someone's advantages or freedom<br><b>Example:</b> The new regulations will clip the wings of aggressive traders.	
Close, But No Cigar	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব কাছাকাছি কিন্তু একদম সঠিক নয়<br><b>English:</b> Very close but not exactly right<br><b>Example:</b> Your guess was 47, the answer is 50 - close, but no cigar.	
Cock and Bull Story	<b>Bengali:</b> বানানো গল্প, সম্ভবত মিথ্যা<br><b>English:</b> Made-up story, probably false<br><b>Example:</b> His excuse about aliens stealing his homework is a cock and bull story.	
Cock-A-Hoop	<b>Bengali:</b> আনন্দিত, উৎসাহিত<br><b>English:</b> Delighted, elated<br><b>Example:</b> She was cock-a-hoop about getting into her dream university.	
Cold Day in Hell	<b>Bengali:</b> অত্যন্ত অসম্ভাব্য ঘটনা<br><b>English:</b> Extremely unlikely event<br><b>Example:</b> It'll be a cold day in hell before he admits he was wrong.	
Come By Something Honestly	<b>Bengali:</b> সৎভাবে অর্জন করা বা উত্তরাধিকারসূত্রে পাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Acquire honestly or inherit<br><b>Example:</b> She came by her musical talent honestly - both parents were musicians.	
Come Clean	<b>Bengali:</b> স্বীকার করা, দোষ মেনে নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Confess, admit guilt<br><b>Example:</b> He finally came clean about breaking the vase.	
Come Hell or High Water	<b>Bengali:</b> যা-ই হোক না কেন<br><b>English:</b> Whatever happens<br><b>Example:</b> Come hell or high water, I'll be at your wedding.	
Come Out in the Wash	<b>Bengali:</b> স্থায়ী ক্ষতি ছাড়াই সমাধান হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Be resolved without permanent damage<br><b>Example:</b> Don't worry about the argument - it will all come out in the wash.	
Come Out of the Closet	<b>Bengali:</b> নিজের গোপন বিষয় প্রকাশ করা<br><b>English:</b> Reveal one's secret matters<br><b>Example:</b> He came out of the closet to his family last year.	
Come Out Swinging	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব আক্রমণাত্মকভাবে জবাব দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Respond very aggressively<br><b>Example:</b> When criticized, the politician came out swinging with harsh accusations.	
Come Rain and Shine	<b>Bengali:</b> যে অবস্থাতেই হোক নিয়মিত করা<br><b>English:</b> Do regularly whatever the conditions<br><b>Example:</b> She walks her dog every morning, come rain and shine.	
Come to Grips With	<b>Bengali:</b> সমস্যা স্বীকার করে তা সমাধানের প্রস্তুতি নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Acknowledge problem and prepare to solve it<br><b>Example:</b> The company needs to come to grips with its financial difficulties.	
Come to Terms With	<b>Bengali:</b> খারাপ কিছু ঘটলে তা মেনে নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Accept something bad that has happened<br><b>Example:</b> It took years for her to come to terms with her father's death.	
Coming Down the Pike	<b>Bengali:</b> নিকট ভবিষ্যতে ঘটার সম্ভাবনা<br><b>English:</b> Likely to happen in the near future<br><b>Example:</b> There are major changes coming down the pike for our department.	
Cook Someone's Goose	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো পরাজয় নিশ্চিত করা<br><b>English:</b> Ensure someone's defeat<br><b>Example:</b> That scandal really cooked his goose - his political career is over.	
Cook Up a Storm	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রচুর খাবার রান্না করা<br><b>English:</b> Cook a large amount of food<br><b>Example:</b> Grandmother always cooks up a storm for family gatherings.	
Cool as A Cucumber	<b>Bengali:</b> কঠিন পরিস্থিতিতেও শান্ত থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Remain calm even in difficult situations<br><b>Example:</b> Even during the crisis, the CEO stayed cool as a cucumber.	
Cool Cat	<b>Bengali:</b> সহজভাবে সম্মান অর্জনকারী<br><b>English:</b> Someone who easily earns respect<br><b>Example:</b> With his smooth style and confidence, he's a real cool cat.	
Cool Your Heels	<b>Bengali:</b> অপেক্ষা করা<br><b>English:</b> Wait<br><b>Example:</b> The doctor is busy - you'll have to cool your heels in the waiting room.	
Couch Potato	<b>Bengali:</b> অলস ব্যক্তি যে অনেক টিভি দেখে<br><b>English:</b> Lazy person who watches a lot of TV<br><b>Example:</b> Since retirement, he's become a couch potato, watching TV all day.	
Crash a Party	<b>Bengali:</b> নিমন্ত্রণ ছাড়া পার্টিতে যোগ দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Attend a party without invitation<br><b>Example:</b> They decided to crash the wedding party next door.	
Crickets	<b>Bengali:</b> নীরবতা<br><b>English:</b> Silence<br><b>Example:</b> When he asked for volunteers, all he heard was crickets.	
Cross to Bear	<b>Bengali:</b> দীর্ঘমেয়াদী সমস্যা, ভারী বোঝা<br><b>English:</b> Long-term problem, heavy burden<br><b>Example:</b> His chronic illness is a cross to bear for the whole family.	
Crunch the Numbers	<b>Bengali:</b> সিদ্ধান্তের আগে গণনা করা<br><b>English:</b> Calculate before making decisions<br><b>Example:</b> Let me crunch the numbers before we decide on the budget.	
Crunch Time	<b>Bengali:</b> চাপের সময়, কঠোর পরিশ্রমের সময়<br><b>English:</b> Pressure time, time for hard work<br><b>Example:</b> It's crunch time - we have only 24 hours to finish the project.	
Cry Over Spilt Milk	<b>Bengali:</b> ঘটে যাওয়া বিষয় নিয়ে দুঃখ করা<br><b>English:</b> Grieve over things that have already happened<br><b>Example:</b> Stop crying over spilt milk - what's done is done.	
Cry Wolf	<b>Bengali:</b> মিথ্যা সতর্কতা দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Give false warnings<br><b>Example:</b> If you keep crying wolf, no one will believe you when there's real danger.	
Cry Your Eyes Out	<b>Bengali:</b> দীর্ঘ সময় জোরে কাঁদা<br><b>English:</b> Cry loudly for a long time<br><b>Example:</b> She cried her eyes out when her dog died.	
Curiosity Killed The Cat	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রশ্ন করা বন্ধ করো, খুব বেশি কৌতূহলী হয়ো না<br><b>English:</b> Stop asking questions, don't be too curious<br><b>Example:</b> Don't ask about her personal life - curiosity killed the cat.	
Cut To the Quick	<b>Bengali:</b> গভীরভাবে আবেগিক আঘাত দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Cause deep emotional hurt<br><b>Example:</b> His harsh criticism cut her to the quick.	
Cut Corners	<b>Bengali:</b> মান কমিয়ে সাশ্রয় করা<br><b>English:</b> Save money by reducing quality<br><b>Example:</b> Don't cut corners on safety equipment to save money.	
Cut It Fine	<b>Bengali:</b> শেষ মুহূর্তে কিছু করা<br><b>English:</b> Do something at the last moment<br><b>Example:</b> Arriving at the airport 30 minutes before departure is cutting it fine.	
Cut Off Your Nose to Spite Your Face	<b>Bengali:</b> গর্বের বশে নিজের ক্ষতি করা<br><b>English:</b> Harm yourself out of pride<br><b>Example:</b> Quitting without another job lined up is cutting off your nose to spite your face.	
Cut Someone Some Slack	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে কঠোরভাবে বিচার না করা<br><b>English:</b> Not judge someone harshly<br><b>Example:</b> Cut him some slack - he's been under a lot of stress lately.	
Cut the Gordian Knot	<b>Bengali:</b> জটিল সমস্যার সহজ সমাধান<br><b>English:</b> Simple solution to a complex problem<br><b>Example:</b> Instead of negotiating for months, he cut the Gordian knot by making a direct offer.	
Cut the Mustard	<b>Bengali:</b> পর্যাপ্তভাবে কিছু করা<br><b>English:</b> Do something adequately<br><b>Example:</b> If you can't cut the mustard in this job, we'll have to let you go.	
Cut to the Chase	<b>Bengali:</b> মূল বিষয়ে আসা<br><b>English:</b> Get to the main point<br><b>Example:</b> Let's cut to the chase - how much will this cost?	
Cut Your Teeth on Something	<b>Bengali:</b> কোনো ক্ষেত্রে প্রাথমিক দক্ষতা অর্জন করা<br><b>English:</b> Gain initial skills in a field<br><b>Example:</b> She cut her teeth on small projects before handling major accounts.	
Cutting-Edge	<b>Bengali:</b> অত্যাধুনিক, উদ্ভাবনী<br><b>English:</b> State-of-the-art, innovative<br><b>Example:</b> This company is known for its cutting-edge technology.	
Dance to Someone's Tune	<b>Bengali:</b> ধারাবাহিকভাবে কারো নির্দেশনা অনুসরণ করা<br><b>English:</b> Consistently follow someone's directions<br><b>Example:</b> The employees are tired of dancing to the boss's tune.	
Dance with the Devil	<b>Bengali:</b> জেনেশুনে অনৈতিক কাজ করা<br><b>English:</b> Knowingly do immoral things<br><b>Example:</b> Getting involved with that corrupt politician is dancing with the devil.	
Dark Horse	<b>Bengali:</b> আশ্চর্যজনক প্রতিযোগী<br><b>English:</b> Surprising competitor<br><b>Example:</b> The unknown candidate was a dark horse who won the election.	
Darken Someone's Door	<b>Bengali:</b> অবাঞ্ছিত সফর করা<br><b>English:</b> Make an unwelcome visit<br><b>Example:</b> Don't ever darken my door again after what you did!	
Dead Ahead	<b>Bengali:</b> সরাসরি সামনে<br><b>English:</b> Straight ahead<br><b>Example:</b> The lighthouse is dead ahead - we're almost at port.	
Dead as the Dodo	<b>Bengali:</b> সম্পূর্ণ বিলুপ্ত<br><b>English:</b> Completely extinct<br><b>Example:</b> That old technology is dead as the dodo now.	
Dead Eye	<b>Bengali:</b> ভালো নিশানাবাজ<br><b>English:</b> Good marksman<br><b>Example:</b> The sniper was a dead eye who never missed his target.	
Dead Heat	<b>Bengali:</b> সমান অবস্থান<br><b>English:</b> Tied position<br><b>Example:</b> The race ended in a dead heat - both runners crossed simultaneously.	
Dead of Winter	<b>Bengali:</b> শীতের সবচেয়ে ঠান্ডা অংশ<br><b>English:</b> The coldest part of winter<br><b>Example:</b> Moving in the dead of winter was a terrible idea.	
Dead ringer	<b>Meaning:</b> Someone or something that looks exactly like another. <br><br> <b>Origin:</b> From horse racing; a 'ringer' was a fast horse substituted for a slow one to cheat. <br><br> <b>Example:</b> He’s a dead ringer for that famous actor.	
Dead Run	<b>Bengali:</b> যতটা দ্রুত সম্ভব দৌড়ানো<br><b>English:</b> Running as fast as possible<br><b>Example:</b> He ran dead run to catch the departing train.	
Dead Shot	<b>Bengali:</b> ভালো নিশানাবাজ<br><b>English:</b> Excellent marksman<br><b>Example:</b> As a dead shot, she won every archery competition.	
Deep Pockets	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রচুর অর্থের মালিক<br><b>English:</b> Having a lot of money<br><b>Example:</b> Only investors with deep pockets can afford this venture.	
Deliver the Goods	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রত্যাশিত জিনিস প্রদান করা<br><b>English:</b> Provide what is expected<br><b>Example:</b> The new employee really delivered the goods on her first project.	
Devil's Advocate	<b>Bengali:</b> বিভিন্ন দৃষ্টিভঙ্গি প্রকাশের জন্য বিপরীত মত দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Present opposing views to explore different perspectives<br><b>Example:</b> Let me play devil's advocate - what if this plan fails?	
Dirty Look	<b>Bengali:</b> অসন্তুষ্টি প্রকাশকারী মুখভাব<br><b>English:</b> Facial expression showing displeasure<br><b>Example:</b> She gave him a dirty look when he interrupted her presentation.	
Do 12-Ounce Curls	<b>Bengali:</b> বিয়ার পান করা<br><b>English:</b> Drinking beer<br><b>Example:</b> After work, he likes to do 12-ounce curls at the local bar.	
Dodge a Bullet	<b>Bengali:</b> অল্পের জন্য বিপদ এড়ানো<br><b>English:</b> Narrowly avoid danger<br><b>Example:</b> By leaving that company before the layoffs, she dodged a bullet.	
Doesn't Amount to a Hill of Beans	<b>Bengali:</b> গুরুত্বহীন, নগণ্য<br><b>English:</b> Unimportant, insignificant<br><b>Example:</b> All his complaints don't amount to a hill of beans.	
Dog Days of the Summer	<b>Bengali:</b> গ্রীষ্মের সবচেয়ে গরম দিন<br><b>English:</b> The hottest days of summer<br><b>Example:</b> During the dog days of summer, everyone stays indoors with air conditioning.	
Dog in the Manger	<b>Bengali:</b> নিজে ব্যবহার না করে অন্যকেও ব্যবহার করতে না দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Not using something yourself but preventing others from using it<br><b>Example:</b> He's being a dog in the manger by hoarding office supplies he doesn't need.	
Dog-and-Pony Show	<b>Bengali:</b> চটকদার উপস্থাপনা<br><b>English:</b> Flashy presentation<br><b>Example:</b> The sales meeting was just a dog-and-pony show with no real substance.	
Dog-Eat-Dog	<b>Bengali:</b> তীব্র প্রতিযোগিতামূলক<br><b>English:</b> Intensely competitive<br><b>Example:</b> The corporate world can be dog-eat-dog when it comes to promotions.	
Don't Cry Over Spilled Milk	<b>Bengali:</b> ছোট বিষয় নিয়ে চিন্তা করো না<br><b>English:</b> Don't worry about small matters<br><b>Example:</b> The glass broke, but don't cry over spilled milk - we can get another one.	
Don't Judge a Book by Its Cover	<b>Bengali:</b> চেহারা দেখে বিচার করো না<br><b>English:</b> Don't judge based on appearance<br><b>Example:</b> He may look rough, but don't judge a book by its cover - he's very kind.	
Don't Look a Gift Horse in the Mouth	<b>Bengali:</b> উপহারের মূল্য নিয়ে প্রশ্ন করো না<br><b>English:</b> Don't question the value of a gift<br><b>Example:</b> The car may be old, but don't look a gift horse in the mouth.	
Double-Dip	<b>Bengali:</b> অনুচিতভাবে দুই উৎস থেকে আয় করা<br><b>English:</b> Inappropriately earn from two sources<br><b>Example:</b> The consultant was double-dipping by working for competing companies.	
Double-Edged Sword	<b>Bengali:</b> সাহায্যকারী এবং ক্ষতিকর দুটোই হতে পারে<br><b>English:</b> Can be both helpful and harmful<br><b>Example:</b> Social media is a double-edged sword - it connects people but can spread misinformation.	
Down in the Dumps	<b>Bengali:</b> বিষণ্ণ, দুঃখিত<br><b>English:</b> Depressed, sad<br><b>Example:</b> She's been down in the dumps since losing her job.	
Down the Road	<b>Bengali:</b> ভবিষ্যতে<br><b>English:</b> In the future<br><b>Example:</b> We might consider expanding down the road when we have more capital.	
Drag One's Feet	<b>Bengali:</b> অনিচ্ছায় ধীরে ধীরে কিছু করা<br><b>English:</b> Do something slowly and reluctantly<br><b>Example:</b> Stop dragging your feet and make a decision about the job offer.	
Drain the Lizard	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রস্রাব করা<br><b>English:</b> Urinate<br><b>Example:</b> Excuse me, I need to drain the lizard before we continue the meeting.	
Draw a Blank	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু মনে করতে পারা না<br><b>English:</b> Unable to remember something<br><b>Example:</b> When asked his name, I drew a complete blank.	
Draw a Line in the Sand	<b>Bengali:</b> চূড়ান্ত সীমা নির্ধারণ করা<br><b>English:</b> Set a final limit<br><b>Example:</b> The manager drew a line in the sand about tardiness - one more late arrival means termination.	
Draw a Line Under	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু সমাপ্ত করে এগিয়ে যাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Finish something and move on<br><b>Example:</b> Let's draw a line under this argument and start fresh.	
Draw a Long Bow	<b>Bengali:</b> বাড়িয়ে বলা, মিথ্যা বলা<br><b>English:</b> Exaggerate, tell lies<br><b>Example:</b> He's drawing a long bow with that fish story - it wasn't that big.	
Draw the Line	<b>Bengali:</b> গ্রহণযোগ্যতার সীমা নির্ধারণ করা<br><b>English:</b> Set limits of acceptability<br><b>Example:</b> I'll help with overtime, but I draw the line at working weekends.	
Dressed Up to the Nines	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব সুন্দর বা আকর্ষণীয় পোশাক পরা<br><b>English:</b> Wearing very elegant or attractive clothes<br><b>Example:</b> She was dressed up to the nines for the gala dinner.	
Drink the Kool-Aid	<b>Bengali:</b> বিপজ্জনক ধারণাগুলো অন্ধভাবে মেনে নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Blindly accept dangerous ideas<br><b>Example:</b> Don't drink the Kool-Aid - think critically about what they're telling you.	
Drive a Hard Bargain	<b>Bengali:</b> কার্যকরভাবে দরকষাকষি করা<br><b>English:</b> Negotiate effectively<br><b>Example:</b> She drives a hard bargain when buying cars - always gets the best price.	
Drive a Wedge Between	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি গ্রুপে বিভেদ সৃষ্টি করা<br><b>English:</b> Create division in a group<br><b>Example:</b> The manager's favoritism drove a wedge between team members.	
Drive Someone Up the Wall	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে গভীরভাবে বিরক্ত করা<br><b>English:</b> Deeply annoy someone<br><b>Example:</b> His constant humming drives me up the wall.	
Drop a Line	<b>Bengali:</b> চিঠি লেখা বা ইমেইল পাঠানো<br><b>English:</b> Write a letter or send an email<br><b>Example:</b> Drop me a line when you arrive safely.	
Drop the Ball	<b>Bengali:</b> দায়িত্ব পালনে ব্যর্থ হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Fail to fulfill responsibility<br><b>Example:</b> The project manager really dropped the ball by missing the deadline.	
Dry Run	<b>Bengali:</b> অনুশীলন<br><b>English:</b> Practice session<br><b>Example:</b> Let's do a dry run of the presentation before the board meeting.	
Dutch Courage	<b>Bengali:</b> সাহস পাওয়ার জন্য মদ্যপান<br><b>English:</b> Drinking alcohol to gain courage<br><b>Example:</b> He needed some Dutch courage before asking for a raise.	
Dutch Uncle	<b>Bengali:</b> অত্যন্ত সমালোচনাপ্রবণ ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> Extremely critical person<br><b>Example:</b> My father-in-law talks to me like a Dutch uncle about my career choices.	
Dyed-In-The-Wool	<b>Bengali:</b> দীর্ঘ সময় ধরে একই মতে অবিচল<br><b>English:</b> Unchanging in the same opinion for a long time<br><b>Example:</b> He's a dyed-in-the-wool conservative who never changes his views.	
Eagle-Eyed	<b>Bengali:</b> তীক্ষ্ণ দৃষ্টি<br><b>English:</b> Sharp vision<br><b>Example:</b> The eagle-eyed editor caught every typo in the manuscript.	
Early Bird	<b>Bengali:</b> যে স্বাভাবিক সময়ের আগে কিছু করে<br><b>English:</b> Someone who does things earlier than normal<br><b>Example:</b> The early bird catches the worm - she arrives at work before everyone else.	
Eat Crow	<b>Bengali:</b> ভুল স্বীকার করে অপমান মেনে নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Accept humiliation by admitting mistakes<br><b>Example:</b> After the prediction failed, the analyst had to eat crow publicly.	
Eat Humble Pie	<b>Bengali:</b> পরাজয় বা ভুল স্বীকার করে অপমান মেনে নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Accept humiliation by admitting defeat or mistakes<br><b>Example:</b> When proven wrong, he had to eat humble pie in front of his colleagues.	
Eat Someone's Lunch	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে পুরোপুরি পরাজিত করা<br><b>English:</b> Completely defeat someone<br><b>Example:</b> The new competitor ate our lunch by offering better prices.	
Eat Your Heart Out	<b>Bengali:</b> ঈর্ষা করো<br><b>English:</b> Be jealous<br><b>Example:</b> Look at my new car - eat your heart out!	
Eighty-Six	<b>Bengali:</b> বাতিল করা বা কাউকে বের করে দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Cancel or remove someone<br><b>Example:</b> The bouncer eighty-sixed the troublemaker from the bar.	
Elephant in the Room	<b>Bengali:</b> যে বড় সমস্যা নিয়ে কেউ কথা বলছে না<br><b>English:</b> Big problem that no one is talking about<br><b>Example:</b> The elephant in the room is that we're running out of money.	
Elevator Music	<b>Bengali:</b> পাবলিক জায়গায় বাজানো মনোরম কিন্তু বিরক্তিকর সঙ্গীত<br><b>English:</b> Pleasant but annoying music played in public places<br><b>Example:</b> The waiting room had boring elevator music playing all day.	
Elevator Pitch	<b>Bengali:</b> সংক্ষিপ্ত উপস্থাপনা<br><b>English:</b> Brief presentation<br><b>Example:</b> You have 30 seconds to give me your elevator pitch about this product.	
Eleventh Hour	<b>Bengali:</b> শেষ মুহূর্ত<br><b>English:</b> Last moment<br><b>Example:</b> He submitted his application at the eleventh hour.	
Even Steven	<b>Bengali:</b> সমান অবস্থা, কোনো ঋণ নেই<br><b>English:</b> Equal status, no debt<br><b>Example:</b> After paying back the loan, we're even steven.	
Every Dog Has His Day	<b>Bengali:</b> সবার একটি গৌরবের মুহূর্ত আসে<br><b>English:</b> Everyone has a moment of glory<br><b>Example:</b> Don't worry about being overlooked now - every dog has his day.	
Every Man and His Dog	<b>Bengali:</b> অনেক মানুষ<br><b>English:</b> Many people<br><b>Example:</b> Every man and his dog was at the concert last night.	
Every Man for Himself	<b>Bengali:</b> নিজের স্বার্থ দেখো, অন্যের সাহায্য আশা করো না<br><b>English:</b> Look after your own interests, don't expect help from others<br><b>Example:</b> When the company started failing, it was every man for himself.	
Excused Boots	<b>Bengali:</b> বাধ্যতামূলক কাজ এড়ানোর অনুমতি<br><b>English:</b> Permission to avoid mandatory tasks<br><b>Example:</b> The injured soldier got excused boots from the morning march.	
Face the Music	<b>Bengali:</b> পরিণতির মুখোমুখি হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Deal with consequences of one's actions<br><b>Example:</b> After cheating on the exam, he had to face the music.	
Fall for Something Hook, Line, and Sinker	<b>Bengali:</b> সম্পূর্ণভাবে প্রতারিত হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Be completely deceived<br><b>Example:</b> She fell for his sob story hook, line, and sinker.	
Fall in Love with Somebody	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো প্রেমে পড়া<br><b>English:</b> Start feeling love towards somebody<br><b>Example:</b> He fell in love with his neighbor at first sight.	
Fall Off the Wagon	<b>Bengali:</b> মদ্যপান ছেড়ে দেওয়ার পর আবার শুরু করা<br><b>English:</b> Resume drinking alcohol after quitting<br><b>Example:</b> After six months sober, he fell off the wagon at the party.	
Fall on One's Sword	<b>Bengali:</b> দোষ স্বীকার করা; আত্মত্যাগ করা<br><b>English:</b> Accept blame; sacrifice oneself<br><b>Example:</b> The manager fell on his sword and resigned after the project failed.	
Fall Prey to	<b>Bengali:</b> শিকার হওয়া; ক্ষতিগ্রস্ত হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Be victimized by; be harmed by<br><b>Example:</b> Many elderly people fall prey to telephone scams.	
Fancy Someone	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে খুব আকর্ষণীয় মনে করা<br><b>English:</b> Find someone very attractive<br><b>Example:</b> I think she fancies the new guy in accounting.	
Farther (On) Down the Road	<b>Bengali:</b> পরবর্তী সময়ে; ভবিষ্যতে<br><b>English:</b> Later, at some unspecified time<br><b>Example:</b> We'll consider expansion farther down the road.	
Fashion-Forward	<b>Bengali:</b> নতুন ফ্যাশন দ্রুত গ্রহণ করে এমন<br><b>English:</b> Tending to adopt new styles quickly<br><b>Example:</b> She's always fashion-forward, wearing the latest trends.	
Fat Cat	<b>Bengali:</b> উচ্চপদস্থ, উচ্চ বেতনভোগী কর্মকর্তা<br><b>English:</b> A highly placed, well-paid executive<br><b>Example:</b> The fat cats on Wall Street got huge bonuses while workers were laid off.	
Father Figure	<b>Bengali:</b> পথপ্রদর্শক; পিতৃতুল্য ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> A mentor, a person who offers guidance<br><b>Example:</b> The coach became a father figure to the young athletes.	
Feast Your Eyes On	<b>Bengali:</b> চোখের তৃপ্তিতে দেখা<br><b>English:</b> Take great pleasure in looking at someone or something<br><b>Example:</b> Feast your eyes on this beautiful sunset!	
Feather in One's Cap	<b>Bengali:</b> গৌরবজনক অর্জন<br><b>English:</b> An achievement for which one is recognized<br><b>Example:</b> Winning the award was a real feather in her cap.	
Feather One's (Own) Nest	<b>Bengali:</b> ক্ষমতা অপব্যবহার করে আর্থিক লাভ করা<br><b>English:</b> Use one's influence or power improperly for financial gain<br><b>Example:</b> The politician was accused of feathering his own nest through insider trading.
