Writing (Handwriting) on the Wall	<b>Bengali:</b> আগামী বিপদের ইঙ্গিত<br><b>English:</b> Hints of coming disaster<br><b>Example:</b> The writing was on the wall - the company was going bankrupt.	
Year In, Year Out	<b>Bengali:</b> বছরের পর বছর একইভাবে<br><b>English:</b> Annually without change<br><b>Example:</b> Year in, year out, he follows the same routine.	
You Can Lead a Horse to Water, but You Can't Make It Drink	<b>Bengali:</b> জোর করে কাউকে দিয়ে কিছু করানো যায় না<br><b>English:</b> It's very hard to force someone to do something against his or her will<br><b>Example:</b> I showed him how to study, but you can lead a horse to water, but you can't make it drink.	
You Can Say That Again!	<b>Bengali:</b> একদম সত্যি কথা!<br><b>English:</b> I agree totally!<br><b>Example:</b> This weather is terrible! - You can say that again!	
You Can Take It to the Bank	<b>Bengali:</b> এটা সম্পূর্ণ নিশ্চিত<br><b>English:</b> I absolutely guarantee this<br><b>Example:</b> She'll be late - you can take it to the bank.	
You Can't Judge a Book by Its Cover	<b>Bengali:</b> বাহ্যিক চেহারা দেখে মানুষকে বোঝা যায় না<br><b>English:</b> You can't know people (or things) well by their external appearances<br><b>Example:</b> He looks rough, but you can't judge a book by its cover.	
You Can't Make an Omelet (Omelette) Without Breaking	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু ত্যাগ ছাড়া সফলতা পাওয়া যায় না<br><b>English:</b> You can't accomplish something without some sacrifice<br><b>Example:</b> Starting a business requires investment - you can't make an omelet without breaking eggs.	
You Can't Make Fish of One and Fowl of the Other	<b>Bengali:</b> সবার সাথে সমান আচরণ করতে হবে<br><b>English:</b> People must be treated equally<br><b>Example:</b> You can't give him special treatment - you can't make fish of one and fowl of the other.	
You Know the Drill	<b>Bengali:</b> তুমি নিয়মটা জানো<br><b>English:</b> You are already familiar with the procedure<br><b>Example:</b> Time for the monthly report - you know the drill.	
You Snooze, You Lose	<b>Bengali:</b> দেরি করলে সুযোগ হাতছাড়া হয়ে যাবে<br><b>English:</b> If you delay or are not alert, you will miss opportunities<br><b>Example:</b> The tickets sold out in minutes - you snooze, you lose.	
Young at Heart	<b>Bengali:</b> বয়স নির্বিশেষে তরুণ মানসিকতা রাখা<br><b>English:</b> Having a youthful outlook, regardless of age<br><b>Example:</b> At 70, she's still young at heart and loves adventure.	
Your Guess Is as Good as Mine	<b>Bengali:</b> আমিও জানি না; আমারও কোনো ধারণা নেই<br><b>English:</b> I don't know; I have no idea<br><b>Example:</b> When will this rain stop? Your guess is as good as mine.	
Your Mileage May Vary	<b>Bengali:</b> তোমার ফলাফল ভিন্ন হতে পারে<br><b>English:</b> You may get different results. This does not necessarily refer to a car, although it may<br><b>Example:</b> This diet worked for me, but your mileage may vary.	
Your Number Is Up	<b>Bengali:</b> তোমার সময় শেষ হয়ে এসেছে<br><b>English:</b> You are going to die (or suffer some bad misfortune or setback)<br><b>Example:</b> When the boss calls you to his office, your number is up.	
You're Driving Me Nuts	<b>Bengali:</b> তুমি আমাকে পাগল করে তুলছো<br><b>English:</b> To make someone giddy or crazy<br><b>Example:</b> Your constant humming is driving me nuts!	
Yours Truly	<b>Bengali:</b> আমি<br><b>English:</b> Me<br><b>Example:</b> Who's going to clean this mess? Yours truly, I suppose.	
Zero In On	<b>Bengali:</b> কোনো কিছুর উপর মনোযোগ দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Focus closely on something; take aim at something<br><b>Example:</b> Let's zero in on the main problem.	
Zig When One Should Be Zagging	<b>Bengali:</b> ভুল পথ বেছে নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> To make an error; to choose an incorrect course<br><b>Example:</b> Investing in that stock was zigging when I should have been zagging.	
Zip One's Lip	"<b>Bengali:</b> চুপ থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Be quiet<br><b>Example:</b> Zip your lip and listen to the instructions.""Stem the Tide"	
Step Up One's Game	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রতিযোগিতায় উন্নতির চেষ্টা করা<br><b>English:</b> Work to advance to a higher level of a competition<br><b>Example:</b> If you want that promotion, you need to step up your game.	
Step Up to the Plate	<b>Bengali:</b> দায়িত্ব নেওয়ার জন্য প্রস্তুত হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Prepare to take action, be the person in a group who takes action<br><b>Example:</b> When the manager quit, someone had to step up to the plate.	
Stick It to the Man	<b>Bengali:</b> কর্তৃপক্ষকে বিরক্ত করা<br><b>English:</b> Do something that frustrates those in authority<br><b>Example:</b> The protesters were trying to stick it to the man.	
Stick Your Nose into Something	<b>Bengali:</b> অন্যের বিষয়ে নাক গলানো<br><b>English:</b> Intrude into something that is not your affair<br><b>Example:</b> Stop sticking your nose into my personal business.	
Sticker Shock	<b>Bengali:</b> দামে চমকে যাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Surprise at the high price of something<br><b>Example:</b> I got sticker shock when I saw the price of that car.	
Stick-in-the-Mud	<b>Bengali:</b> নতুন ধারণায় অনীহা<br><b>English:</b> A person who dislikes or adapts slowly to new ideas<br><b>Example:</b> Don't be such a stick-in-the-mud - try something new!	
Sticky Wicket	<b>Bengali:</b> কঠিন পরিস্থিতি<br><b>English:</b> A difficult, tricky situation<br><b>Example:</b> Explaining the layoffs to employees will be a sticky wicket.	
Stiff-Necked	<b>Bengali:</b> জেদী; অতিরিক্ত আনুষ্ঠানিক<br><b>English:</b> Stubborn; excessively formal<br><b>Example:</b> The stiff-necked bureaucrat refused to bend the rules.	
Storm in a Teacup	<b>Bengali:</b> তুচ্ছ বিষয়ে বড় হৈচৈ<br><b>English:</b> A commotion that dies down quickly, about something unimportant<br><b>Example:</b> The controversy over the dress code was a storm in a teacup.	
Stormy Relationship	<b>Bengali:</b> ঝগড়াঝাটিপূর্ণ সম্পর্ক<br><b>English:</b> Relationship that has a lot arguments and disagreement<br><b>Example:</b> They have a stormy relationship but somehow make it work.	
Stumbling Block	<b>Bengali:</b> বাধা<br><b>English:</b> An obstacle, physical or abstract<br><b>Example:</b> Lack of funding is the main stumbling block to the project.	
Straight Arrow	<b>Bengali:</b> সৎ ও বিশ্বস্ত ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> An honest, trustworthy person<br><b>Example:</b> You can trust him - he's a straight arrow.	
Strain at a Gnat and Swallow a Camel	<b>Bengali:</b> ছোট বিষয়ে হৈচৈ, বড় বিষয় উপেক্ষা<br><b>English:</b> To make a fuss over something unimportant while ignoring larger issues<br><b>Example:</b> Worrying about grammar while ignoring the main argument is straining at a gnat and swallowing a camel.	
Strike A Chord	<b>Bengali:</b> পরিচিত লাগা, মনে পড়া<br><b>English:</b> Used to describe something that is familiar to you, reminds you of something or is connected to you somehow<br><b>Example:</b> Her story about growing up poor struck a chord with me.	
Sugar Daddy	<b>Bengali:</b> ধনী পুরুষ যে তরুণীদের অর্থ দেয়<br><b>English:</b> A rich man who is generous with younger women in return for sexual favors<br><b>Example:</b> She's dating that old millionaire - he's obviously her sugar daddy.	
Sure-Fire	<b>Bengali:</b> নিশ্চিত<br><b>English:</b> Certain to occur<br><b>Example:</b> This marketing strategy is a sure-fire way to increase sales.	
Swan Song	<b>Bengali:</b> শেষ কাজ<br><b>English:</b> This expression is used to describe a final act before dying or ending something<br><b>Example:</b> The conductor's performance was his swan song before retirement.	
Sweep Under the Carpet	<b>Bengali:</b> সমস্যা লুকানোর চেষ্টা<br><b>English:</b> Attempt to temporarily conceal a problem or error<br><b>Example:</b> Don't sweep this scandal under the carpet - address it openly.	
Sweet Dreams!	<b>Bengali:</b> ভালো ঘুম হোক!<br><b>English:</b> Sleep well!<br><b>Example:</b> Good night, honey - sweet dreams!	
Sweeten the Deal	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রস্তাবে আকর্ষণীয় কিছু যোগ করা<br><b>English:</b> Add something to an offer during a negotiation<br><b>Example:</b> To sweeten the deal, they threw in free shipping.	
Sweeten the Pot	<b>Bengali:</b> জয়ের পরিমাণ বাড়ানো<br><b>English:</b> Increase the amount of winnings potentially available in a game of chance, especially poker<br><b>Example:</b> The casino sweetened the pot to attract more players.	
Swim Against the Tide	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রচলিত ধারার বিপরীতে যাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Do something contrary to a trend or usual opinion<br><b>Example:</b> He swims against the tide by investing in unpopular stocks.	
Swim with Sharks	<b>Bengali:</b> বড় ঝুঁকি নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> To take a major risk<br><b>Example:</b> Starting a business is like swimming with sharks.	
Swim with the Fishes	<b>Bengali:</b> মারা যাওয়া, বিশেষত অপরাধ জগতে<br><b>English:</b> Have been killed, especially with involvement of organized crime<br><b>Example:</b> Cross the mob boss and you'll swim with the fishes.	
Swing for the Fences	<b>Bengali:</b> সর্বোচ্চ অর্জনের চেষ্টা<br><b>English:</b> Attempt to achieve the largest accomplishment possible<br><b>Example:</b> With this new product, we're swinging for the fences.	
Sword of Damocles	<b>Bengali:</b> ক্রমাগত হুমকির অনুভূতি<br><b>English:</b> Something that causes a feeling of constant threat<br><b>Example:</b> The possibility of layoffs hangs like a sword of Damocles over the office.	
Take (Someone) to the Cleaners	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রতারণা করা; সম্পূর্ণ পরাজয়<br><b>English:</b> Swindle; defeat badly<br><b>Example:</b> The casino took him to the cleaners - he lost everything.	
Take a Deep Dive (Into)	<b>Bengali:</b> গভীরভাবে অনুসন্ধান করা<br><b>English:</b> Explore something extensively<br><b>Example:</b> Let's take a deep dive into the sales data.	
Take a Flyer	<b>Bengali:</b> ঝুঁকিপূর্ণ বিনিয়োগ<br><b>English:</b> To take a rise; especially to make a speculative investment<br><b>Example:</b> He took a flyer on that startup and made millions.	
Take a Gander	<b>Bengali:</b> একনজর দেখা<br><b>English:</b> Go to take a look at something<br><b>Example:</b> Take a gander at this beautiful sunset.	
Take a Hike	<b>Bengali:</b> চলে যাও<br><b>English:</b> Go away<br><b>Example:</b> When he kept bothering me, I told him to take a hike.	
Take A Powder	<b>Bengali:</b> কঠিন পরিস্থিতি এড়াতে চলে যাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> To leave, especially in order to avoid a difficult situation<br><b>Example:</b> When the police arrived, the suspect took a powder.	
Take a Rain Check	<b>Bengali:</b> পরে গ্রহণের প্রতিশ্রুতি দিয়ে প্রস্তাব প্রত্যাখ্যান<br><b>English:</b> Decline an invitation but suggest that you'll accept it at a later time<br><b>Example:</b> I can't make dinner tonight, but can I take a rain check?	
Take Five (Ten)	<b>Bengali:</b> পাঁচ (দশ) মিনিটের বিরতি<br><b>English:</b> Take a short break of five (ten) minutes<br><b>Example:</b> We've been working for hours - let's take five.	
Take It Easy	<b>Bengali:</b> তাড়াহুড়ো করো না; শান্ত থাকো<br><b>English:</b> Don't hurry; relax; don't get angry<br><b>Example:</b> Take it easy - there's no need to rush.	
Take It on The Chin	<b>Bengali:</b> আক্রমণের শিকার হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Be attacked; suffer an attack<br><b>Example:</b> When the scandal broke, he took it on the chin like a man.	
Take It or Leave It	<b>Bengali:</b> হয় নাও, না হয় ছাড়ো<br><b>English:</b> You must decide now whether you will accept this proposal<br><b>Example:</b> That's my final offer - take it or leave it.	
Take Someone to Task	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে কঠোরভাবে তিরস্কার করা<br><b>English:</b> Reprimand someone strongly<br><b>Example:</b> The teacher took the student to task for cheating.	
Take Something with a Pinch of Salt	<b>Bengali:</b> সন্দেহের সাথে গ্রহণ করা<br><b>English:</b> If you take what someone says with a pinch of salt, you do not completely believe it<br><b>Example:</b> Take his fishing stories with a pinch of salt.	
Take the Cake	<b>Bengali:</b> সবচেয়ে চরম উদাহরণ<br><b>English:</b> Be the most extreme instance<br><b>Example:</b> Of all his rude comments, that one takes the cake.	
Take the Edge Off	<b>Bengali:</b> নেতিবাচক কিছুকে সামান্য উন্নত করা<br><b>English:</b> To slightly improve something negative<br><b>Example:</b> A glass of wine will take the edge off after this stressful day.	
Take the Fifth	<b>Bengali:</b> উত্তর দিতে অস্বীকার করা<br><b>English:</b> Refuse to answer because answering might incriminate or cause problems for you<br><b>Example:</b> When questioned about the missing money, he took the fifth.	
Take the Gloves Off	<b>Bengali:</b> আক্রমণাত্মকভাবে আলোচনা করা<br><b>English:</b> Negotiate in a more aggressive way<br><b>Example:</b> The negotiations got serious when both sides took the gloves off.	
Take the High Road	<b>Bengali:</b> নৈতিক উচ্চতা বজায় রাখা<br><b>English:</b> Refuse to descend to immoral activities or personal attacks<br><b>Example:</b> Despite the provocation, she took the high road.	
Take The Mickey (Piss) Out Of Someone	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে নিয়ে মজা করা<br><b>English:</b> Make fun of or ridicule someone<br><b>Example:</b> Stop taking the mickey out of his accent.	
Take the Shine Off	<b>Bengali:</b> ইতিবাচক ঘটনার উজ্জ্বলতা কমানো<br><b>English:</b> To do something that diminishes a positive event<br><b>Example:</b> The rain took the shine off our picnic.	
Take the Starch out of Someone	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো আত্মবিশ্বাস কমানো<br><b>English:</b> Make someone less confident or less arrogant<br><b>Example:</b> That failure really took the starch out of him.	
Take The Wind Out of Someone's Sails	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো উৎসাহ কমিয়ে দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> To reduce someone's confidence, often by doing something unexpected<br><b>Example:</b> Her criticism took the wind out of his sails.	
Take Your Life in Your Hands	<b>Bengali:</b> চরম ঝুঁকি নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Undergo extreme risk<br><b>Example:</b> Driving in this storm is taking your life in your hands.	
Take Your Medicine	<b>Bengali:</b> অপ্রীতিকর কিছু মেনে নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Accept something unpleasant, for example, punishment, without protesting or complaining<br><b>Example:</b> You made the mistake, now take your medicine.	
Take Your Time	<b>Bengali:</b> তাড়াহুড়ো করো না<br><b>English:</b> Don't hurry, work at a relaxed pace<br><b>Example:</b> Take your time with that decision - it's important.	
Taste of Your Own Medicine	<b>Bengali:</b> নিজের কৃতকর্মের ফল ভোগ করা<br><b>English:</b> The same unpleasant experience or treatment that one has given to others<br><b>Example:</b> Now he's getting a taste of his own medicine.	
Teach an Old Dog New Tricks	<b>Bengali:</b> পুরানো অভ্যাস পরিবর্তন করা (সাধারণত নেতিবাচক)<br><b>English:</b> To change someone's long-established habits. Usually used in the negative<br><b>Example:</b> You can't teach an old dog new tricks - he's set in his ways.	
Tear One's Hair out	<b>Bengali:</b> অত্যন্ত চিন্তিত বা হতাশ হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Be extremely worried or frustrated<br><b>Example:</b> This math problem is making me tear my hair out.	
Tear-Jerker	<b>Bengali:</b> কান্নার উদ্রেক করে এমন সিনেমা/বই<br><b>English:</b> A film or book that makes you cry<br><b>Example:</b> That movie was a real tear-jerker - I cried for an hour.	
Tee Many Martoonies	<b>Bengali:</b> অতিরিক্ত মদ্যপান<br><b>English:</b> Too many martinis, scrambled to suggest drunkenness<br><b>Example:</b> He clearly had tee many martoonies at the party.	
Tell It to the Marines	<b>Bengali:</b> আমি বিশ্বাস করি না<br><b>English:</b> I don't believe you; you must think I'm gullible<br><b>Example:</b> You won the lottery? Tell it to the marines!	
Tempest in a Teapot	<b>Bengali:</b> তুচ্ছ বিষয়ে বড় হৈচৈ<br><b>English:</b> A commotion about something unimportant<br><b>Example:</b> The argument over parking spaces was a tempest in a teapot.	
Ten a Penny	<b>Bengali:</b> সাধারণ, সস্তা<br><b>English:</b> Ordinary, inexpensive<br><b>Example:</b> Good programmers aren't ten a penny - they're valuable.	
Ten to One	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব সম্ভাব্য<br><b>English:</b> Something very likely<br><b>Example:</b> Ten to one he'll be late again.	
Test the Waters	<b>Bengali:</b> সাবধানে পরীক্ষা করা<br><b>English:</b> Experiment with something cautiously<br><b>Example:</b> Before investing heavily, let's test the waters with a small amount.	
Thank God It's Friday (TGIF)	<b>Bengali:</b> সপ্তাহের কাজ শেষ হওয়ায় খুশি হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Let's be happy that the workweek is over!<br><b>Example:</b> TGIF - I'm so ready for the weekend!	
That Ship Has Sailed	<b>Bengali:</b> সেই সুযোগ চলে গেছে<br><b>English:</b> That opportunity has passed<br><b>Example:</b> You wanted to invest in Bitcoin at $100? That ship has sailed.	
That's Music to My Ears	<b>Bengali:</b> এটা শুনে আমি খুব খুশি<br><b>English:</b> I am very happy to hear this<br><b>Example:</b> You got the job? That's music to my ears!	
That's a Stretch	<b>Bengali:</b> তুমি যা বলছো তা বিশ্বাস করা কঠিন<br><b>English:</b> What you are suggesting is very difficult to believe; I am very skeptical<br><b>Example:</b> He claims he ran a marathon in two hours? That's a stretch.	
That's All She Wrote	<b>Bengali:</b> গল্পের শেষ<br><b>English:</b> That was the end of the story<br><b>Example:</b> The engine died and that's all she wrote for our road trip.	
The Apple Never Falls Far From the Tree	<b>Bengali:</b> পারিবারিক বৈশিষ্ট্য সাধারণত উত্তরাধিকার সূত্রে পাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Family characteristics are usually inherited<br><b>Example:</b> Like father, like son - the apple never falls far from the tree.	
The Birds and the Bees	<b>Bengali:</b> মানুষের যৌনতা এবং প্রজনন<br><b>English:</b> Human sexuality and reproduction<br><b>Example:</b> It's time we had a talk about the birds and the bees.	
The Cat Is Out of the Bag	<b>Bengali:</b> গোপন কথা ফাঁস হয়ে গেছে<br><b>English:</b> The secret has been revealed<br><b>Example:</b> Well, the cat is out of the bag about the merger.	
The Coast Is Clear	<b>Bengali:</b> আমরা অলক্ষিত; এগিয়ে যাওয়া নিরাপদ<br><b>English:</b> We are unobserved; it is safe to proceed<br><b>Example:</b> The coast is clear - let's sneak into the kitchen.	
The Cherry On the Cake	<b>Bengali:</b> যা কিছুকে নিখুঁত করে তোলে<br><b>English:</b> The final thing that makes something perfect<br><b>Example:</b> Getting promoted was great, but the bonus was the cherry on the cake.	
The Deck Is (The Cards Are): Stacked Against You	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রতিকূল পরিস্থিতি বিদ্যমান<br><b>English:</b> Unfavorable conditions exist<br><b>Example:</b> With his background, the deck is stacked against him.	
The Jig Is Up	<b>Bengali:</b> গোপন অবৈধ কার্যকলাপ ফাঁস; তোমার প্রতারণা শেষ<br><b>English:</b> A secret illicit activity has been exposed; your trickery is finished<br><b>Example:</b> When the police arrived, he knew the jig was up.	
The More Things Change, The More They Stay The Same	<b>Bengali:</b> যদিও কিছু নতুন মনে হতে পারে, মূল পরিস্থিতি অপরিবর্তিত<br><b>English:</b> Although something may seem superficially new, it has not altered the basic situation<br><b>Example:</b> New management, same problems - the more things change, the more they stay the same.	
The Only Game in Town	<b>Bengali:</b> কোনো বিশেষ সেবার একমাত্র বিকল্প<br><b>English:</b> The sole option for a particular service<br><b>Example:</b> This hospital is the only game in town for emergency care.	
The Powers That Be	<b>Bengali:</b> ক্ষমতাসীন ব্যক্তিরা<br><b>English:</b> People in charge, often used when the speaker does not want to identify them<br><b>Example:</b> The powers that be decided to cancel the project.	
The Real McCoy	<b>Bengali:</b> আসল জিনিস<br><b>English:</b> A genuine item<br><b>Example:</b> This isn't a fake - it's the real McCoy.	
The Story Has Legs	<b>Bengali:</b> গল্পটি মানুষের দৃষ্টি আকর্ষণ করছে<br><b>English:</b> People are continuing to pay attention to the story<br><b>Example:</b> This scandal has legs - it'll be in the news for weeks.	
The Time is Ripe	<b>Bengali:</b> উপযুক্ত সময়<br><b>English:</b> If you say that the time is ripe, you mean that it is a suitable point for a particular activity<br><b>Example:</b> The time is ripe for investing in renewable energy.	
The Walls Have Ears	<b>Bengali:</b> আমাদের কথা শোনা হতে পারে; সাবধানে কথা বলো<br><b>English:</b> We may be overheard; be careful what you say<br><b>Example:</b> Lower your voice - the walls have ears in this office.	
The Whole Enchilada	<b>Bengali:</b> সম্পূর্ণ কিছু<br><b>English:</b> All of something<br><b>Example:</b> When I buy a car, I want the whole enchilada - all the options.	
The Whole Shebang	<b>Bengali:</b> সবকিছু, কোনো কিছুর সব অংশ<br><b>English:</b> Everything, all the parts of something<br><b>Example:</b> We're renovating the kitchen - the whole shebang.	
The World Is Your Oyster	<b>Bengali:</b> তোমার অনেক সুযোগ এবং পছন্দ আছে<br><b>English:</b> You have many opportunities and choices<br><b>Example:</b> With your talent and education, the world is your oyster.	
There But For The Grace Of God Go I	<b>Bengali:</b> আমিও সহজেই সেই কাজ করতে পারতাম<br><b>English:</b> I could easily have done what that person did<br><b>Example:</b> Seeing the homeless man, I thought 'there but for the grace of God go I.'	
There's More Than One Way to Skin a Cat	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি লক্ষ্য অর্জনের একাধিক উপায় আছে<br><b>English:</b> There's more than one way of achieving a certain goal<br><b>Example:</b> If that approach doesn't work, don't worry - there's more than one way to skin a cat.	
There's No Such Thing as a Free Lunch	<b>Bengali:</b> বিনামূল্যে কিছুই পাওয়া যায় না<br><b>English:</b> Nothing is given to you without some expectation of something in return<br><b>Example:</b> He's offering to help, but there's no such thing as a free lunch.	
Thin On The Ground	<b>Bengali:</b> বিরল, কদাচিৎ দেখা যায়<br><b>English:</b> Rare, seldom encountered<br><b>Example:</b> Good employees are thin on the ground these days.	
Think Big	<b>Bengali:</b> উচ্চাভিলাষী পরিকল্পনা করা<br><b>English:</b> Consider ambitious plans; avoid becoming overly concerned with details<br><b>Example:</b> Don't limit yourself - think big!	
Think Outside the Box	<b>Bengali:</b> সৃজনশীলভাবে চিন্তা করা<br><b>English:</b> Try to solve a problem in an original way; think creatively<br><b>Example:</b> We need to think outside the box to solve this problem.	
Think Tank	<b>Bengali:</b> বিশেষজ্ঞদের গবেষণা দল<br><b>English:</b> A group of experts engaged in ongoing studies of a particular subject<br><b>Example:</b> The government consulted a think tank about economic policy.	
Third Rail	<b>Bengali:</b> এত সংবেদনশীল বিষয় যা উত্থাপন করা বিপজ্জনক<br><b>English:</b> A topic so sensitive that it is dangerous to raise<br><b>Example:</b> Social Security is the third rail of American politics.	
Third Time's a Charm	<b>Bengali:</b> তৃতীয়বারে সফল হওয়ার সম্ভাবনা<br><b>English:</b> Even if you fail at something twice, you may well succeed the third time<br><b>Example:</b> I failed the driving test twice, but third time's a charm!	
Thirty-Thousand-Foot View	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব বিস্তৃত বা সাধারণ দৃষ্টিভঙ্গি<br><b>English:</b> A very broad or general perspective<br><b>Example:</b> Let me give you the thirty-thousand-foot view of our strategy.	
This Has (Person X) Written All Over It	<b>Bengali:</b> এটা অমুকের জন্য একদম উপযুক্ত<br><b>English:</b> [Person X] would really like or be well suited to this<br><b>Example:</b> This art project has Sarah written all over it.	
This Is Not Your Father's ____	<b>Bengali:</b> এই জিনিসটি আগের চেয়ে অনেক উন্নত<br><b>English:</b> This item has been much updated from its earlier versions<br><b>Example:</b> This is not your father's Buick - it's completely redesigned.	
Three Sheets to the Wind	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব মাতাল<br><b>English:</b> Very drunk<br><b>Example:</b> By the end of the party, he was three sheets to the wind.	
Through the Grapevine	<b>Bengali:</b> গুজবের মাধ্যমে<br><b>English:</b> Via gossip<br><b>Example:</b> I heard through the grapevine that you're getting married.	
Through Thick and Thin	<b>Bengali:</b> ভালো এবং খারাপ সময়ে<br><b>English:</b> In good times and bad<br><b>Example:</b> She stood by him through thick and thin.	
Throw a Wet Blanket on (Something)	<b>Bengali:</b> কোনো পরিকল্পনায় নিরুৎসাহিত করা<br><b>English:</b> Discourage plans for something<br><b>Example:</b> Don't throw a wet blanket on our vacation plans.	
Throw a Wrench Into	<b>Bengali:</b> নাশকতা করা; ব্যর্থ করা<br><b>English:</b> To sabotage; to cause to fail<br><b>Example:</b> The strike threw a wrench into our production schedule.	
Throw Caution to the Wind	<b>Bengali:</b> সাহসিকতার সাথে কাজ করা, বিবেচনা ছাড়া<br><b>English:</b> To act in a daring way, without forethought<br><b>Example:</b> He threw caution to the wind and quit his job to travel.	
Throw Down the Gauntlet	"<b>Bengali:</b> চ্যালেঞ্জ ছুড়ে দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> To issue a challenge<br><b>Example:</b> TheRing a Bell"""	duplicate
Rob Peter to Pay Paul	<b>Bengali:</b> এক ঋণ শোধ করতে আরেক ঋণ নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Pay off a debt with another loan; solve a problem in such a way that it leads to a new problem<br><b>Example:</b> Using credit cards to pay mortgage is robbing Peter to pay Paul.	
Rob the Cradle	<b>Bengali:</b> বয়সে অনেক ছোট কারো সাথে সম্পর্ক<br><b>English:</b> To be sexually or romantically involved with someone who is very young<br><b>Example:</b> At 45, dating a 22-year-old is really robbing the cradle.	
Rock Bottom	<b>Bengali:</b> একেবারে নিচু অবস্থা<br><b>English:</b> An absolute low point<br><b>Example:</b> After losing his job and home, he hit rock bottom.	
Rock the Boat	<b>Bengali:</b> গোষ্ঠীতে বিশৃঙ্খলা সৃষ্টি করা<br><b>English:</b> Cause a disruption in a group<br><b>Example:</b> Don't rock the boat - things are going well as they are.	
Roll the Dice On	<b>Bengali:</b> ঝুঁকি নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Take a risk<br><b>Example:</b> We're rolling the dice on this new product launch.	
Roll With the Punches	<b>Bengali:</b> নমনীয় হয়ে সমস্যার মোকাবিলা করা<br><b>English:</b> Deal with problems by being flexible<br><b>Example:</b> Business is unpredictable - you have to roll with the punches.	
Rome Wasn't Built in a Day	<b>Bengali:</b> জটিল কাজে সময় লাগে<br><b>English:</b> Complex projects take time<br><b>Example:</b> Learning a language takes practice - Rome wasn't built in a day.	
Rookie Mistake	<b>Bengali:</b> নতুনদের ভুল<br><b>English:</b> An error made by an inexperienced person<br><b>Example:</b> Forgetting to save your work is a rookie mistake.	
Rotten to the Core	<b>Bengali:</b> সম্পূর্ণ পচা/খারাপ<br><b>English:</b> Entirely evil<br><b>Example:</b> That corrupt politician is rotten to the core.	
Rub (Something) in Someone's Face	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো ভুল বারবার উল্লেখ করে অপমান করা<br><b>English:</b> Humiliate someone by repeating and criticizing his or her mistake<br><b>Example:</b> Stop rubbing my failure in my face - I get it.	
Rub It In	<b>Bengali:</b> ভুলের জন্য আরো খারাপ বোধ করানো<br><b>English:</b> Say something that makes someone feel even worse about a mistake<br><b>Example:</b> I know I messed up - you don't have to rub it in.	
Rub Someone's Nose in (Something)	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো ভুল ঘষে ঘষে মনে করিয়ে দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Humiliate someone by repeating and criticizing his or her mistake<br><b>Example:</b> He keeps rubbing my nose in that old mistake.	
Rubber-Stamp	<b>Bengali:</b> বিবেচনা ছাড়াই অনুমোদন দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Approve something without consideration, as a formality<br><b>Example:</b> The board just rubber-stamped the CEO's proposal.	
Rule of Thumb	<b>Bengali:</b> সাধারণ নিয়ম বা নির্দেশনা<br><b>English:</b> A general principle or guideline, not a specific formula<br><b>Example:</b> The rule of thumb is to save 10% of your income.	
Run a Tight Ship	<b>Bengali:</b> কঠোরভাবে সংস্থা পরিচালনা করা<br><b>English:</b> Manage an organization in a strict, well-regulated way<br><b>Example:</b> The new principal runs a tight ship - no nonsense allowed.	
Run in the Family	<b>Bengali:</b> পারিবারিক বৈশিষ্ট্য<br><b>English:</b> Be inherited (as a trait) by multiple members of a family<br><b>Example:</b> Musical talent runs in their family.	
Run into a Buzz Saw	<b>Bengali:</b> অপ্রত্যাশিত গুরুতর সমস্যায় পড়া<br><b>English:</b> Encounter severe and unexpected problems<br><b>Example:</b> The new policy ran into a buzz saw of opposition.	
Run off at the Mouth	<b>Bengali:</b> অপ্রয়োজনীয় কথা বলা<br><b>English:</b> Talk a lot about unimportant things, talk incoherently<br><b>Example:</b> He tends to run off at the mouth when he's nervous.	
Run on Fumes	<b>Bengali:</b> শক্তি বা সম্পদ প্রায় শেষ<br><b>English:</b> To be in a situation where one's energy or resources is almost exhausted<br><b>Example:</b> After working 16 hours, I'm running on fumes.	
Run Out of Steam	<b>Bengali:</b> গতি হারানো, ক্লান্ত হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Lose momentum, become tired<br><b>Example:</b> The protest movement ran out of steam after a few weeks.	
Run the Table	<b>Bengali:</b> সব খেলায় জয়ী হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Win every game or contest<br><b>Example:</b> The team ran the table in the playoffs.	
Sacred Cow	<b>Bengali:</b> যার সমালোচনা করা যায় না<br><b>English:</b> An individual or organization that one cannot criticize<br><b>Example:</b> The old professor is a sacred cow - no one dares question his methods.	
Saving Grace	<b>Bengali:</b> খারাপ পরিস্থিতি থেকে রক্ষাকারী বিষয়<br><b>English:</b> Something that redeems a bad situation<br><b>Example:</b> The only saving grace of that terrible movie was the soundtrack.	
Scare the Living Daylights Out of Someone	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে ভীষণ ভয় পাওয়ানো<br><b>English:</b> Frighten someone severely<br><b>Example:</b> That horror movie scared the living daylights out of me.	
Scorched Earth	<b>Bengali:</b> নির্দয়, অত্যন্ত ধ্বংসাত্মক<br><b>English:</b> Ruthless, extremely destructive<br><b>Example:</b> The company used scorched earth tactics against its competitors.	
Screw The Pooch	<b>Bengali:</b> গুরুতর ভুল করা<br><b>English:</b> To make a serious error<br><b>Example:</b> I really screwed the pooch on that presentation.	
School Of Hard Knocks	<b>Bengali:</b> কঠিন জীবনের অভিজ্ঞতা<br><b>English:</b> Difficult real-life experiences from which one has learned<br><b>Example:</b> He didn't go to college - he graduated from the school of hard knocks.	
Second Banana	<b>Bengali:</b> অধীনস্থ ব্যক্তি<br><b>English:</b> A person in a subservient position<br><b>Example:</b> He's tired of being second banana to his more successful brother.	
Second Stringer	<b>Bengali:</b> বিকল্প খেলোয়াড়<br><b>English:</b> A substitute player in a sport; a substitute for a job who is not the most talented person<br><b>Example:</b> After the injury, the second stringer had to play.	
Second Wind	<b>Bengali:</b> নতুন শক্তি<br><b>English:</b> Renewed energy<br><b>Example:</b> After resting briefly, the runner got her second wind.	
See Eye to Eye	<b>Bengali:</b> একমত হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> To concur, agree<br><b>Example:</b> We don't always see eye to eye, but we respect each other.	
See Something Out of the Corner of Your Eye	<b>Bengali:</b> চোখের কোনা দিয়ে দেখা<br><b>English:</b> Use peripheral vision<br><b>Example:</b> I saw the car coming out of the corner of my eye.	
Seize the Bull By the Horns	<b>Bengali:</b> সমস্যার সরাসরি মোকাবিলা করা<br><b>English:</b> Attack a problem directly<br><b>Example:</b> It's time to seize the bull by the horns and address this issue.	
Seize the Day	<b>Bengali:</b> সুযোগ গ্রহণ করা<br><b>English:</b> Take an opportunity<br><b>Example:</b> Life is short - seize the day and follow your dreams.	
Sell (Someone) a Bill of Goods	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে প্রতারণা করা<br><b>English:</b> Trick someone; be deceptive<br><b>Example:</b> The salesman sold me a bill of goods about that car.	
Sell Like Hotcakes	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব দ্রুত বিক্রি হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Be sold very quickly<br><b>Example:</b> The new iPhone is selling like hotcakes.	
Selling Point	<b>Bengali:</b> আকর্ষণীয় বৈশিষ্ট্য<br><b>English:</b> An attractive feature of something for sale<br><b>Example:</b> The main selling point of this house is its location.	
Set in Stone	<b>Bengali:</b> অপরিবর্তনীয়<br><b>English:</b> Fixed; unchangeable<br><b>Example:</b> The schedule isn't set in stone - we can make changes.	
Set something to Music	<b>Bengali:</b> কথার সাথে সুর যোগ করা<br><b>English:</b> To write a piece of music to accompany a set of words<br><b>Example:</b> The composer set the poem to music beautifully.	
Set the Bar (Too) High	<b>Bengali:</b> উচ্চ মান নির্ধারণ করা<br><b>English:</b> To set a high standard for something<br><b>Example:</b> Don't set the bar too high for new employees.	
Set the Thames on Fire	<b>Bengali:</b> অসাধারণ কিছু করা (সাধারণত নেতিবাচক)<br><b>English:</b> Do something amazing. Usually used in the negative<br><b>Example:</b> He's competent, but he'll never set the Thames on fire.	
Set the World on Fire	<b>Bengali:</b> অসাধারণ কিছু করা<br><b>English:</b> Do something amazing; have a brilliant stretch in one's career<br><b>Example:</b> The young entrepreneur is setting the world on fire with her innovations.	
Shake the Dust off Your Shoes	<b>Bengali:</b> সম্পর্ক বা পরিস্থিতির সাথে পুরোপুরি ছেদ<br><b>English:</b> Make a clean break with a relationship or situation<br><b>Example:</b> After the toxic job, I shook the dust off my shoes and moved on.	
Shape Up or Ship Out	<b>Bengali:</b> ঠিক হও না হলে চলে যাও<br><b>English:</b> Behave properly or leave the organization<br><b>Example:</b> The coach told the lazy players to shape up or ship out.	
Sharp as A Tack	<b>Bengali:</b> মানসিকভাবে তীক্ষ্ণ<br><b>English:</b> Mentally agile<br><b>Example:</b> Despite being 90, my grandmother is still sharp as a tack.	
Shell Game	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রতারণার পদ্ধতি<br><b>English:</b> A method of deception in which you conceal your actions by moving something frequently<br><b>Example:</b> The company's accounting was a shell game to hide losses.	
Shift Gears	<b>Bengali:</b> বিষয় পরিবর্তন করা<br><b>English:</b> Change the subject, or change what one is doing<br><b>Example:</b> Let's shift gears and talk about something more pleasant.	
Shipshape And Bristol Fashion	<b>Bengali:</b> পরিচ্ছন্ন ও গোছানো<br><b>English:</b> Tidy, clean<br><b>Example:</b> The admiral wants everything shipshape and Bristol fashion.	
Shit a Brick	<b>Bengali:</b> অত্যন্ত ভীত হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Be extremely fearful<br><b>Example:</b> I nearly shit a brick when I saw the spider.	
Shoot from the Hip	<b>Bengali:</b> বিবেচনা ছাড়াই কাজ করা<br><b>English:</b> Talk or act without consideration<br><b>Example:</b> He tends to shoot from the hip in meetings.	
Shoot Off One's Mouth	<b>Bengali:</b> অবিবেচক কথা বলা<br><b>English:</b> Talk without considering one's words<br><b>Example:</b> He shot off his mouth and revealed confidential information.	
Shoot Oneself In The Foot	<b>Bengali:</b> নিজের ক্ষতি করা<br><b>English:</b> Do something that damages oneself or one's own cause<br><b>Example:</b> By lying to the boss, he shot himself in the foot.	
Short Fuse	<b>Bengali:</b> দ্রুত রেগে যাওয়ার প্রবণতা<br><b>English:</b> A quick temper; a tendency to anger quickly<br><b>Example:</b> Be careful around him - he has a short fuse.	
Shot Across the Bow	<b>Bengali:</b> আরো গুরুতর পদক্ষেপের সতর্কবাণী<br><b>English:</b> A warning of more serious actions to come<br><b>Example:</b> The lawsuit was just a shot across the bow.	
Show Me an X And I'll Show You a Y	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রতিটি কাজের পরিণতি আছে<br><b>English:</b> There is a consequence to X that you may not have thought of<br><b>Example:</b> Show me a successful person and I'll show you someone who works hard.	
Show One's True Colors	<b>Bengali:</b> আসল চরিত্র প্রকাশ করা<br><b>English:</b> Reveal one's true nature<br><b>Example:</b> When the pressure mounted, he showed his true colors.	
Show Your Cards	<b>Bengali:</b> পরিকল্পনা প্রকাশ করা<br><b>English:</b> Reveal your resources or plans<br><b>Example:</b> Don't show your cards too early in the negotiation.	
Sick and Tired of	<b>Bengali:</b> কোনো পুনরাবৃত্তিমূলক বিষয়ে বিরক্ত<br><b>English:</b> Extremely annoyed by something that occurs repeatedly<br><b>Example:</b> I'm sick and tired of your constant complaints.	
Sick as a Dog	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব অসুস্থ<br><b>English:</b> Extremely ill<br><b>Example:</b> I was sick as a dog with the flu last week.	
Sick as a Parrot	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব হতাশ<br><b>English:</b> Very disappointed<br><b>Example:</b> When his team lost, he was sick as a parrot.	
Sight for Sore Eyes	<b>Bengali:</b> আনন্দদায়ক দৃশ্য<br><b>English:</b> A sight that makes you happy<br><b>Example:</b> After being away for months, home was a sight for sore eyes.	
Silver Bullet	<b>Bengali:</b> কঠিন সমস্যার সহজ সমাধান<br><b>English:</b> Something simple that resolves a difficult problem<br><b>Example:</b> There's no silver bullet for poverty - it requires multiple solutions.	
Simmer Down	<b>Bengali:</b> রাগ কমানো<br><b>English:</b> Become less angry; regain one's composure<br><b>Example:</b> Simmer down and tell me what happened calmly.	
Sink or Swim	<b>Bengali:</b> ব্যর্থ বা সফল হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Fail or succeed<br><b>Example:</b> At this company, it's sink or swim from day one.	
Sing a Different Tune	<b>Bengali:</b> মতামত পরিবর্তন করা<br><b>English:</b> Change your opinion<br><b>Example:</b> He's singing a different tune now that he knows the facts.	
Sit On (Something)	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু প্রকাশ বা কাজ করতে দেরি করা<br><b>English:</b> Delay revealing or acting on something<br><b>Example:</b> The editor sat on the story for weeks before publishing it.	
Sit Tight	<b>Bengali:</b> অপেক্ষা করা<br><b>English:</b> Wait and do not go anywhere<br><b>Example:</b> Sit tight while I check on the test results.	
Sitting Duck	<b>Bengali:</b> সহজ লক্ষ্য<br><b>English:</b> Something or someone easily attacked or criticized<br><b>Example:</b> Without bodyguards, the celebrity was a sitting duck.	
Sitting Pretty	<b>Bengali:</b> সুবিধাজনক অবস্থানে<br><b>English:</b> In a favorable situation<br><b>Example:</b> With his trust fund, he's sitting pretty for life.	
Six Feet Under	<b>Bengali:</b> মৃত ও সমাহিত<br><b>English:</b> Dead and buried<br><b>Example:</b> The old king is six feet under in the royal cemetery.	
Six of One, a Half Dozen of the Other	<b>Bengali:</b> দুটি পছন্দে কোনো বড় পার্থক্য নেই<br><b>English:</b> The two choices have no significant differences<br><b>Example:</b> Taking the bus or the train? It's six of one, half dozen of the other.	
Six Ways to Sunday	<b>Bengali:</b> সব সম্ভাব্য উপায়ে<br><b>English:</b> In every possible way<br><b>Example:</b> We analyzed the problem six ways to Sunday.	
Slam Dunk	<b>Bengali:</b> নিশ্চিত সফলতা<br><b>English:</b> An effort that is certain to succeed<br><b>Example:</b> Getting the contract should be a slam dunk with our proposal.	
Sleep Like a Baby	<b>Bengali:</b> গভীর ঘুম<br><b>English:</b> To experience a very deep and restful sleep; to sleep soundly<br><b>Example:</b> After the long hike, I slept like a baby.	
Sleep with the Fishes	<b>Bengali:</b> মৃত, প্রায়ই হত্যার মাধ্যমে<br><b>English:</b> Dead, often by murder<br><b>Example:</b> Cross the mafia and you'll sleep with the fishes.	
Slip Someone a Mickey	<b>Bengali:</b> পানীয়ে ওষুধ মিশিয়ে অজ্ঞান করা<br><b>English:</b> Add a drug to an alcoholic drink in order to knock someone out<br><b>Example:</b> Someone slipped her a mickey at the party.	
Slippery Slope	<b>Bengali:</b> বিপজ্জনক ধারাবাহিক পরিণতি<br><b>English:</b> A series of undesirable effects that, one warns, could result from a certain action<br><b>Example:</b> Allowing this exception could be a slippery slope.	
Slower than Molasses	<b>Bengali:</b> অত্যন্ত ধীর<br><b>English:</b> Exceptionally slow or sluggish; not fast at all<br><b>Example:</b> The internet connection is slower than molasses today.	
Small Beer	<b>Bengali:</b> গুরুত্বহীন<br><b>English:</b> Unimportant, insignificant<br><b>Example:</b> Losing five dollars is small beer compared to your salary.	
Small Fry	<b>Bengali:</b> কম প্রভাবশালী মানুষ; শিশুরা<br><b>English:</b> People or organizations with little influence; children<br><b>Example:</b> Don't worry about the competition - they're just small fry.	
Small Potatoes	<b>Bengali:</b> তুচ্ছ বিষয়<br><b>English:</b> Unimportant, insignificant<br><b>Example:</b> A thousand dollars sounds like small potatoes to a millionaire.	
Smell a Rat	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রতারণার সন্দেহ করা<br><b>English:</b> Suspect deception<br><b>Example:</b> When the deal seemed too good to be true, I smelled a rat.	
Smoking Gun	<b>Bengali:</b> অপরাধের নির্ভুল প্রমাণ<br><b>English:</b> Indisputable evidence of a crime<br><b>Example:</b> The email was the smoking gun that proved his guilt.	
Snafu	<b>Bengali:</b> গোলযোগপূর্ণ অবস্থা<br><b>English:</b> A malfunction; a chaotic situation<br><b>Example:</b> The computer upgrade turned into a complete snafu.	
Snake Oil	<b>Bengali:</b> নকল ওষুধ, অকার্যকর সমাধান<br><b>English:</b> A useless medicine; a quack remedy; a product or measure promoted as a solution that really does nothing to help<br><b>Example:</b> That weight loss pill is pure snake oil.	
Sneak Peek	<b>Bengali:</b> আগাম দেখার সুযোগ<br><b>English:</b> A sneak peek is an opportunity to view something in advance of its official opening or debut<br><b>Example:</b> The director gave us a sneak peek of the new movie.	
Soak Up the Sun	<b>Bengali:</b> রোদ উপভোগ করা<br><b>English:</b> To enjoy the sun<br><b>Example:</b> We spent the afternoon soaking up the sun at the beach.	
Sold On (Something)	<b>Bengali:</b> কোনো বিষয়ে নিশ্চিত<br><b>English:</b> Convinced of something<br><b>Example:</b> After the demo, I'm sold on this new software.	
Son of a Gun	<b>Bengali:</b> দুষ্টু ব্যক্তি; বিস্ময়সূচক শব্দ<br><b>English:</b> A rogue. An exclamation of surprise<br><b>Example:</b> Well, I'll be a son of a gun - look who's here!	
Sore Point	<b>Bengali:</b> স্পর্শকাতর বিষয়<br><b>English:</b> A sensitive topic for a particular person<br><b>Example:</b> Don't mention his ex-wife - that's a sore point.	
Sour Grapes	<b>Bengali:</b> হতাশায় লক্ষ্যকে ছোট করে দেখা<br><b>English:</b> Spiteful disparagment of a goal one has failed to achieve<br><b>Example:</b> His criticism of the award is just sour grapes.	
Spare The Rod And Spoil The Child	<b>Bengali:</b> শাসন না করলে সন্তান নষ্ট হয়<br><b>English:</b> It is necessary to physically punish children in order to raise them right<br><b>Example:</b> My grandfather believed in 'spare the rod and spoil the child.'	
Speak of the Devil	<b>Bengali:</b> যার কথা বলছিলাম সে এসে গেছে<br><b>English:</b> The person we have just been talking about has entered<br><b>Example:</b> Speak of the devil - here comes John now!	
Speak with A Plum in One's Mouth	<b>Bengali:</b> উঁচু শ্রেণীর মতো কথা বলা<br><b>English:</b> To speak in a manner that is indicative of a high social class<br><b>Example:</b> She speaks with a plum in her mouth, trying to sound aristocratic.	
Spick and Span	<b>Bengali:</b> পরিচ্ছন্ন ও গোছানো<br><b>English:</b> Clean and neat<br><b>Example:</b> The house was spick and span for the guests' arrival.	
Spill the Beans	<b>Bengali:</b> গোপন কথা ফাঁস করা<br><b>English:</b> Reveal a secret<br><b>Example:</b> Don't spill the beans about the surprise party.	
Spin A Yarn	<b>Bengali:</b> গল্প বলা<br><b>English:</b> Tell a story<br><b>Example:</b> The old sailor loved to spin yarns about his adventures.	
Spin One's Wheels	<b>Bengali:</b> অকার্যকর কাজে ব্যস্ত থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Engaging in activity that yields no progress; getting nowhere<br><b>Example:</b> I've been spinning my wheels on this project all day.	
Spit into The Wind	<b>Bengali:</b> অর্থহীন কাজে সময় নষ্ট<br><b>English:</b> Wasting time on something futile<br><b>Example:</b> Arguing with him is like spitting into the wind.	
Spoiling for a Fight	<b>Bengali:</b> লড়াইয়ের জন্য উদ্গ্রীব<br><b>English:</b> Combative, wanting conflict, eager to argue or fight<br><b>Example:</b> He's been spoiling for a fight all evening.	
Square the Circle	<b>Bengali:</b> অসম্ভব কাজের চেষ্টা<br><b>English:</b> Attempt an impossible task<br><b>Example:</b> Trying to please everyone is like squaring the circle.	
Stab Someone in the Back	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো সাথে বিশ্বাসঘাতকতা করা<br><b>English:</b> To betray (somebody)<br><b>Example:</b> I trusted him, but he stabbed me in the back.	
Stalking Horse	<b>Bengali:</b> পরীক্ষামূলক প্রার্থী<br><b>English:</b> Someone who tests a concept in advance of its application; a candidate who enters a political race in order to test the strength of the incumbent<br><b>Example:</b> Many suspected he was just a stalking horse for the real candidate.	
Stand (Someone) In Good Stead	<b>Bengali:</b> ভবিষ্যতে কাজে আসা<br><b>English:</b> Be useful in the future<br><b>Example:</b> Your college education will stand you in good stead.	
Stand On One's Own Two Feet	<b>Bengali:</b> স্বনির্ভর হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> To be independent and self-sufficient<br><b>Example:</b> It's time for you to stand on your own two feet.	
Stand One's Ground	<b>Bengali:</b> নিজের অবস্থানে অটল থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Refuse to back down; insist on one's position<br><b>Example:</b> Despite the pressure, she stood her ground.	
Start with a Clean Slate	<b>Bengali:</b> নতুন করে শুরু করা<br><b>English:</b> To start (something) again with a fresh beginning; to work on a problem without thinking about what has been done before<br><b>Example:</b> Let's start with a clean slate and forget past mistakes.	
Steal Someone's Thunder	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো গুরুত্ব কমিয়ে দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Upstage someone<br><b>Example:</b> She stole his thunder by announcing her engagement at his party.	
Stem the Tide	"<b>Bengali:</b> অনিষ্টকর কিছুর বৃদ্ধি রোধ করা<br><b>English:</b> To stop or control the growth of something, usually something unpleasant<br><b>Example:</b> The government tried to stem the tide of unemployment.""Pushing Up Daisies"	
Put a Thumb on the Scale	<b>Bengali:</b> অন্যায়ভাবে আলোচনায় প্রভাব বিস্তার করার চেষ্টা, প্রতারণা করা<br><b>English:</b> Try to influence a discussion in an unfair way, cheat<br><b>Example:</b> The judge put a thumb on the scale by favoring one side.	
Put Down Roots	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি জায়গায় নিজেকে প্রতিষ্ঠিত করা; বসতি স্থাপন করা<br><b>English:</b> Establish oneself in a place; settle<br><b>Example:</b> After years of traveling, they decided to put down roots in Portland.	
Put in One's Two Cents	<b>Bengali:</b> আপনার মতামত বলা<br><b>English:</b> Say your opinion<br><b>Example:</b> If I may put in my two cents, I think we should postpone the meeting.	
Put Lipstick on a Pig	<b>Bengali:</b> খারাপ কিছুতে বাহ্যিক পরিবর্তন করা<br><b>English:</b> Make cosmetic changes to something bad<br><b>Example:</b> Repainting the old car is just putting lipstick on a pig.	
Put one's Face On	<b>Bengali:</b> সাজসজ্জা করা<br><b>English:</b> Apply cosmetics<br><b>Example:</b> Give me five minutes to put my face on before we leave.	
Put Out Feelers	<b>Bengali:</b> বিচক্ষণ, অনানুষ্ঠানিক পরামর্শ দেওয়া, খোঁজখবর নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Make discreet, informal suggestions, ask around<br><b>Example:</b> I'm putting out feelers about job opportunities in other companies.	
Put Someone on the Spot	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে অবিলম্বে একটি প্রশ্নের উত্তর দিতে বা সিদ্ধান্ত নিতে বাধ্য করা<br><b>English:</b> Force someone to answer a question or make a decision immediately<br><b>Example:</b> The reporter put the politician on the spot with that tough question.	
Put That in Your Pipe and Smoke It	<b>Bengali:</b> আমি যা বলছি তা গ্রহণ করুন এবং বিবেচনা করুন, যদিও আপনার পছন্দ না হয়!<br><b>English:</b> Accept and consider what I'm saying, even if you don't like it!<br><b>Example:</b> I got the promotion you wanted - put that in your pipe and smoke it!	
Put the Best Face On (Something)	<b>Bengali:</b> খারাপ পরিস্থিতির ইতিবাচক দিকগুলির উপর জোর দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Emphasize the positive aspects of a bad situation<br><b>Example:</b> Despite the layoffs, the CEO tried to put the best face on the company's restructuring.	
Put the Brakes On	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু ধীর করে দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Slow something down<br><b>Example:</b> The board put the brakes on the expansion plans.	
Put the Cart Before the Horse	<b>Bengali:</b> সঠিক ক্রমের বাইরে কিছু করা<br><b>English:</b> To do things out of the proper order<br><b>Example:</b> Buying furniture before finding an apartment is putting the cart before the horse.	
Put the Cat Among The Pigeons	<b>Bengali:</b> এমন কিছু বলা বা করা যা সমস্যা বা বিতর্ক সৃষ্টি করে<br><b>English:</b> Say or do something that causes trouble or controversy<br><b>Example:</b> Mentioning budget cuts put the cat among the pigeons at the staff meeting.	
Put the Genie Back in the Bottle	<b>Bengali:</b> ইতিমধ্যে প্রকাশিত বা সম্পন্ন হওয়া কিছু দমন করার চেষ্টা করা<br><b>English:</b> Try to suppress something that has already been revealed or done<br><b>Example:</b> Once the scandal broke, there was no putting the genie back in the bottle.	
Put the Pedal to the Metal	<b>Bengali:</b> যত দ্রুত সম্ভব গাড়ি চালানো<br><b>English:</b> Drive as fast as possible<br><b>Example:</b> We're late - put the pedal to the metal!	
Put Up with (Something)	<b>Bengali:</b> সহ্য করা, মেনে নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Tolerate, accept<br><b>Example:</b> I won't put up with this rude behavior anymore.	
Put Words Into Someone's Mouth	<b>Bengali:</b> এমন কারো কাছে মতামত আরোপ করা যে কখনো সেই মতামত ব্যক্ত করেনি<br><b>English:</b> Attributing an opinion to someone who has never stated that opinion<br><b>Example:</b> Don't put words into my mouth - I never said I agreed with that plan.	
Put Your Foot Down	<b>Bengali:</b> নেতিবাচক আচরণ বন্ধ করতে আপনার কর্তৃত্ব ব্যবহার করা<br><b>English:</b> Use your authority to stop negative behavior<br><b>Example:</b> When the kids got too rowdy, mom put her foot down.	
Put Your Foot In Your Mouth	<b>Bengali:</b> এমন কিছু বলা যা আপনি অবিলম্বে অনুশোচনা করেন<br><b>English:</b> Say something that you immediately regret<br><b>Example:</b> I put my foot in my mouth when I asked about her ex-husband at the party.	
Put Your Money Where Your Mouth Is	<b>Bengali:</b> আর্থিক প্রতিশ্রুতি দিয়ে আপনার মতামতকে সমর্থন করা<br><b>English:</b> Back up your opinions with a financial commitment<br><b>Example:</b> You say this stock will rise? Put your money where your mouth is and buy some.	
Quake In One's Boots	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব ভয় পাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> To be very frightened<br><b>Example:</b> The thought of giving that presentation makes me quake in my boots.	
Quarter Past	<b>Bengali:</b> ঘন্টার পর পনেরো মিনিট<br><b>English:</b> Fifteen minutes after the hour<br><b>Example:</b> The meeting starts at quarter past two.	
Quarter To/Of	<b>Bengali:</b> ঘন্টার আগে পনেরো মিনিট<br><b>English:</b> Fifteen minutes before the hour<br><b>Example:</b> I'll meet you at quarter to five.	
Queer the Pitch	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো পরিকল্পনায় বাধা দেওয়া; কিছু কঠিন করে তোলা<br><b>English:</b> Interfere with someone's plans; make something more difficult<br><b>Example:</b> The rain queered the pitch for our outdoor wedding.	
Quick as a Flash	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব দ্রুত<br><b>English:</b> Very fast<br><b>Example:</b> Quick as a flash, the cat caught the mouse.	
Quick-and-Dirty	<b>Bengali:</b> আনুমানিক, তাড়াহুড়ো করে করা<br><b>English:</b> Approximate, hastily done<br><b>Example:</b> I need a quick-and-dirty estimate of the costs.	
Quote Unquote	<b>Bengali:</b> ব্যঙ্গাত্মকভাবে বলা<br><b>English:</b> Ironically speaking; suggesting that if a phrase were written out, it would be in quotation marks to convey sarcasm<br><b>Example:</b> He's a quote unquote expert, but he doesn't know much.	
Race Against Time	<b>Bengali:</b> সময়ের বিরুদ্ধে দৌড়, নির্দিষ্ট সময়ে শেষ করার জন্য তাড়াহুড়ো করা<br><b>English:</b> To rush to meet a deadline, to be forced to do something very quickly<br><b>Example:</b> It's a race against time to finish the project before the deadline.	
Rain Cats And Dogs	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রবল বৃষ্টি হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Rain heavily<br><b>Example:</b> It's raining cats and dogs - we should stay inside.	
Rain on Someone's Parade	<b>Bengali:</b> কারো পরিকল্পনা নষ্ট করা<br><b>English:</b> Spoil someone's plans<br><b>Example:</b> I don't want to rain on your parade, but that idea won't work.	
Raise (Someone's) Hackles	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে রাগান্বিত ও প্রতিরক্ষামূলক করে তোলা<br><b>English:</b> Make someone angry and defensive<br><b>Example:</b> His arrogant comments raised everyone's hackles.	
Raise One's Voice	<b>Bengali:</b> জোরে কথা বলা<br><b>English:</b> Talk loudly<br><b>Example:</b> There's no need to raise your voice - I can hear you perfectly.	
Raise Red Flags	<b>Bengali:</b> আগাম বিপদের সতর্কতা দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Warn of trouble ahead<br><b>Example:</b> His evasive answers raised red flags during the interview.	
Raise the Bar	<b>Bengali:</b> মান বৃদ্ধি করা<br><b>English:</b> Increase standards in a certain competition or area of endeavor<br><b>Example:</b> The new coach raised the bar for athletic performance.	
Raise the Roof	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব চিৎকার-চেঁচামেচি করা<br><b>English:</b> Make a great deal of noise (said of a crowd)<br><b>Example:</b> The fans raised the roof when their team scored.	
Rake (Someone) Over the Coals	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে কঠোরভাবে তিরস্কার করা<br><b>English:</b> To scold someone severely<br><b>Example:</b> The boss raked him over the coals for the accounting error.	
Rake Over the Ashes	<b>Bengali:</b> পুরানো বিতর্ক নতুন করে শুরু করা<br><b>English:</b> Restart a settled argument; examine a failure<br><b>Example:</b> Let's not rake over the ashes of last year's problems.	
Rank and File	<b>Bengali:</b> সংস্থার সাধারণ সদস্যরা<br><b>English:</b> The ordinary members of an organization<br><b>Example:</b> The decision wasn't popular with the rank and file.	
Read Between the Lines	<b>Bengali:</b> লুকানো অর্থ বুঝে নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Perceive what is not explicitly stated<br><b>Example:</b> You need to read between the lines to understand what she really means.	
Read the Tea Leaves	<b>Bengali:</b> ছোট লক্ষণ দেখে ভবিষ্যৎ অনুমান করা<br><b>English:</b> Predict the future from small signs<br><b>Example:</b> Political analysts are reading the tea leaves from the latest polls.	
Rear Its Ugly Head	<b>Bengali:</b> সমস্যা বা অপ্রীতিকর কিছু প্রকাশ পাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Appear, be revealed (said of a problem or something unpleasant)<br><b>Example:</b> The corruption scandal reared its ugly head again.	
Rearrange the Deck Chairs on the Titanic	<b>Bengali:</b> বড় সমস্যা উপেক্ষা করে তুচ্ছ কাজে ব্যস্ত থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Taking superficial actions while ignoring a much larger and perhaps fatal problem<br><b>Example:</b> Fixing the office decorations while the company goes bankrupt is like rearranging deck chairs on the Titanic.	
Red Flag	<b>Bengali:</b> সতর্কবাণী, বিপদের লক্ষণ<br><b>English:</b> A warning; a sign of trouble ahead<br><b>Example:</b> His reluctance to discuss finances was a red flag.	
Red Herring	<b>Bengali:</b> বিভ্রান্তিকর সূত্র<br><b>English:</b> A misleading clue; something intended to mislead<br><b>Example:</b> The detective realized the bloody knife was just a red herring.	
Red Meat	<b>Bengali:</b> রাজনৈতিক উস্কানিমূলক বক্তব্য<br><b>English:</b> Political appeals designed to excite one's core supporters; demagoguery<br><b>Example:</b> The politician threw red meat to his base with inflammatory statements.	
Red Tape	<b>Bengali:</b> আমলাতান্ত্রিক জটিলতা<br><b>English:</b> Bureaucracy; difficult bureaucratic or governmental requirements<br><b>Example:</b> Getting a permit involves so much red tape.	
Red-Light District	<b>Bengali:</b> পতিতালয় এলাকা<br><b>English:</b> A neighborhood with many houses of prostitution<br><b>Example:</b> Tourists are warned to avoid the red-light district at night.	
Reinvent the Wheel	<b>Bengali:</b> যার সমাধান আছে তার জন্য নতুন সমাধান খোঁজা<br><b>English:</b> Devise a solution to a problem for which a solution already exists<br><b>Example:</b> Don't reinvent the wheel - use the existing template.	
Riding High	<b>Bengali:</b> সাফল্যের শীর্ষে থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Enjoying success<br><b>Example:</b> After the big contract, the company is riding high.	
Right as Rain	<b>Bengali:</b> সম্পূর্ণ সঠিক<br><b>English:</b> Absolutely correct<br><b>Example:</b> Your analysis of the problem is right as rain.	
Right Under (One's) Nose	<b>Bengali:</b> সামনেই থাকা কিন্তু লক্ষ্য না করা<br><b>English:</b> In an obvious location, yet overlooked<br><b>Example:</b> The keys were right under my nose the whole time.	
Right-Hand Man	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রধান সহায়ক<br><b>English:</b> Chief assistant<br><b>Example:</b> She's the CEO's right-hand man in all major decisions.	
Ring a Bell	<b>Bengali:</b> পরিচিত লাগা<br><b>English:</b> Sound familiar<br><b>Example:</b> That name rings a bell, but I can't place where I've heard it.	
"No Love Lost Between"""	<b>Bengali:</b> দুজনের মধ্যে পারস্পরিক শত্রুতা আছে<br><b>English:</b> There is a mutual animosity between two people<br><b>Example:</b> There's no love lost between those two former partners.	
No Names, No Pack Drill	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে চিহ্নিত করা না গেলে কেউ শাস্তি পাবে না<br><b>English:</b> If no one can be identified, no one will be punished<br><b>Example:</b> I heard someone was stealing from the petty cash, but no names, no pack drill.	
No Rhyme or Reason (to)	<b>Bengali:</b> যুক্তি বা প্যাটার্ন ছাড়া<br><b>English:</b> Without logic or pattern<br><b>Example:</b> There's no rhyme or reason to his decision-making process.	
No Room to Swing A Cat	<b>Bengali:</b> খুবই ছোট, যথেষ্ট বড় নয়<br><b>English:</b> Very small, not big enough<br><b>Example:</b> The apartment is tiny - no room to swing a cat.	
No Shit, Sherlock	<b>Bengali:</b> এটা খুবই স্পষ্ট!<br><b>English:</b> That's very obvious!<br><b>Example:</b> You figured out that water is wet? No shit, Sherlock!	
No Tree Grows to the Sky	<b>Bengali:</b> বৃদ্ধি অনির্দিষ্টকাল ধরে চলতে পারে না<br><b>English:</b> Growth cannot continue indefinitely<br><b>Example:</b> The stock market boom won't last forever - no tree grows to the sky.	
Not Cut Out for (Something)	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু ভালভাবে করার জন্য প্রাকৃতিকভাবে যথেষ্ট দক্ষ নয়<br><b>English:</b> Not naturally skillful enough to do something well<br><b>Example:</b> He's just not cut out for sales - too shy and introverted.	
Not Enough Room to Swing a Cat	<b>Bengali:</b> খুবই ছোট স্থান<br><b>English:</b> A very small space<br><b>Example:</b> This office cubicle doesn't have enough room to swing a cat.	
Not Give A Fig	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু সম্পর্কে একেবারেই চিন্তা না করা<br><b>English:</b> To not care at all about something<br><b>Example:</b> I don't give a fig what people think about my hair.	
Not Have A Cat In Hell's Chance	<b>Bengali:</b> সফল হওয়া, ঘটা, বা কিছু অর্জনের কোন সম্ভাবনা নেই<br><b>English:</b> Have no possibility of succeeding, coming to pass, or achieving something<br><b>Example:</b> He doesn't have a cat in hell's chance of winning that race.	
Not Have a Prayer	<b>Bengali:</b> সফলতার কোন সুযোগ নেই<br><b>English:</b> Have no chance of success<br><b>Example:</b> Against that experienced team, we don't have a prayer.	
Not Know Jack	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছুই জানা নেই<br><b>English:</b> Not know anything<br><b>Example:</b> When it comes to car engines, I don't know jack.	
Not Lift a Finger	<b>Bengali:</b> সাহায্য করতে কিছুই না করা<br><b>English:</b> Do nothing to help<br><b>Example:</b> While we cleaned the house, he didn't lift a finger to help.	
Not Mince Words	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি বিবৃতি মধ্যপন্থী বা দুর্বল করা<br><b>English:</b> Moderate or weaken a statement<br><b>Example:</b> I won't mince words - your performance has been terrible.	
Not One's Cup of Tea	<b>Bengali:</b> যে বিষয়ে আগ্রহ নেই<br><b>English:</b> Not something one is interested in<br><b>Example:</b> Opera isn't my cup of tea - I prefer rock concerts.	
Not Playing with A Full Deck	<b>Bengali:</b> বোকা, মানসিকভাবে ঘাটতিযুক্ত বা প্রতিবন্ধী<br><b>English:</b> Stupid, mentally deficient or impaired<br><b>Example:</b> Anyone who believes that conspiracy theory isn't playing with a full deck.	
Not Ready for Prime Time	<b>Bengali:</b> এখনো নিখুঁত নয়; অভিজ্ঞতাহীন<br><b>English:</b> Not yet perfected; inexperienced<br><b>Example:</b> The new software isn't ready for prime time - it has too many bugs.	
Not Sit Well with (Someone)	<b>Bengali:</b> গ্রহণ করা কঠিন; কাউকে অস্বস্তিকর করা<br><b>English:</b> Be difficult to accept; make someone uncomfortable<br><b>Example:</b> His rude behavior doesn't sit well with me.	
Nothing to Write Home About	<b>Bengali:</b> অসাধারণ নয়, সাধারণ<br><b>English:</b> Unspectacular, ordinary<br><b>Example:</b> The movie was okay, but nothing to write home about.	
Nuts and Bolts	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছুর দৈনন্দিন বিস্তারিত<br><b>English:</b> Everyday details of something<br><b>Example:</b> Let's discuss the nuts and bolts of the project implementation.	
Nutty as a Fruitcake	<b>Bengali:</b> পাগল; বোকা; উদ্ভট<br><b>English:</b> Crazy; idiotic; wacky<br><b>Example:</b> My neighbor is nutty as a fruitcake - he talks to his garden gnomes.	
Pack Heat	<b>Bengali:</b> বন্দুক বহন করা<br><b>English:</b> Carry a gun<br><b>Example:</b> In that dangerous neighborhood, many people pack heat for protection.	
Paddle One's Own Canoe	<b>Bengali:</b> স্বাধীনভাবে কাজ করতে সক্ষম হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> To be able to act independently<br><b>Example:</b> Since graduating, she's learned to paddle her own canoe.	
Page-Turner	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি উত্তেজনাপূর্ণ বই যা পড়তে সহজ, একটি বই যা রাখা কঠিন<br><b>English:</b> A page-turner is an exciting book that's easy to read, a book that's difficult to put down<br><b>Example:</b> That mystery novel was a real page-turner - I finished it in one sitting.	
Pain in the Ass	<b>Bengali:</b> যে কেউ বা কিছু আপনার জীবনকে কঠিন করে তুলছে<br><b>English:</b> Someone or something making your life difficult<br><b>Example:</b> Filing taxes is such a pain in the ass every year.	
Paint the Town Red	<b>Bengali:</b> পানীয় এবং পার্টির জন্য বাইরে যাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Go out drinking and partying<br><b>Example:</b> After finals, the students painted the town red.	
Par for the Course	<b>Bengali:</b> যা সাধারণত প্রত্যাশিত হবে। এর নেতিবাচক অর্থ আছে<br><b>English:</b> What would normally be expected. This has a negative connotation<br><b>Example:</b> Traffic jams during rush hour are par for the course in this city.	
Pass the Buck	<b>Bengali:</b> সমস্যা অন্য কারো কাছে স্থানান্তর করা<br><b>English:</b> Transfer a problem to someone else<br><b>Example:</b> Don't pass the buck - take responsibility for your mistake.	
Pass With Flying Colors	<b>Bengali:</b> উজ্জ্বলভাবে সফল হওয়া, যেমন পরীক্ষা বা অন্য পরীক্ষায়<br><b>English:</b> To succeed brilliantly, as on an exam or other test<br><b>Example:</b> She passed her driving test with flying colors.	
Passing Fancy	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি অস্থায়ী আগ্রহ বা আকর্ষণ<br><b>English:</b> A temporary interest or attraction<br><b>Example:</b> His interest in photography was just a passing fancy.	
Pay Through the Nose (For Something)	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রচুর অর্থ প্রদান করা<br><b>English:</b> Pay a large amount of money<br><b>Example:</b> We paid through the nose for those concert tickets.	
Peaches and Cream	<b>Bengali:</b> এমন পরিস্থিতি, প্রক্রিয়া, ইত্যাদি যার কোনো সমস্যা বা অসুবিধা নেই<br><b>English:</b> A situation, process, etc., that has no trouble or problems<br><b>Example:</b> Marriage isn't always peaches and cream - it takes work.	
Pecking Order	<b>Bengali:</b> স্তরবিন্যাস, গুরুত্বের ক্রম<br><b>English:</b> Hierarchy, rank of importance<br><b>Example:</b> In the corporate pecking order, she ranks quite high.	
Pencil Something In	<b>Bengali:</b> অস্থায়ী ব্যবস্থা করা<br><b>English:</b> Make tentative arrangements<br><b>Example:</b> Let me pencil you in for lunch next Tuesday.	
Penny-Pinching	<b>Bengali:</b> মিতব্যয়ী, যখনই সম্ভব খরচ এড়ানো<br><b>English:</b> Frugal, avoiding expenses whenever possible<br><b>Example:</b> His penny-pinching ways helped him save for retirement.	
Pep Talk	<b>Bengali:</b> একজন ব্যক্তি বা গ্রুপের কাছে উৎসাহব্যঞ্জক বক্তৃতা<br><b>English:</b> An encouraging speech given to a person or group<br><b>Example:</b> The coach gave the team a pep talk before the big game.	
Perfect Storm	<b>Bengali:</b> বিপর্যয়কর ঘটনার একটি বিরল সমন্বয়<br><b>English:</b> A rare combination of disastrous occurrences<br><b>Example:</b> The company's failure was a perfect storm of bad management and market conditions.	
Pet Peeve	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি ছোট জিনিস যা আপনি বিশেষভাবে বিরক্তিকর মনে করেন<br><b>English:</b> A small thing that you find particularly annoying<br><b>Example:</b> My biggest pet peeve is people who are always late.	
Pick a Fight	<b>Bengali:</b> ইচ্ছাকৃতভাবে কারো সাথে দ্বন্দ্ব বা লড়াই উস্কে দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Intentionally provoke a conflict or fight with someone<br><b>Example:</b> He's always trying to pick a fight with his coworkers.	
Pick Up the Slack	<b>Bengali:</b> অন্য কেউ যা করছে না তা করা; অন্য কারো দায়িত্ব গ্রহণ করা<br><b>English:</b> Do something that someone else is not doing; assume someone else's responsibilities<br><b>Example:</b> When John quit, the rest of us had to pick up the slack.	
Pick Up the Tab	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি গ্রুপের কাছে উপস্থাপিত বিল পরিশোধ করা, বিশেষ করে রেস্তোরাঁ বা বারে<br><b>English:</b> To pay a bill presented to a group, especially in a restaurant or bar<br><b>Example:</b> Don't worry about dinner - the company will pick up the tab.	
Pie in the Sky	<b>Bengali:</b> এমন কিছু যা অবাস্তব বা অর্জন করা যায় না<br><b>English:</b> Something that is unrealistic or that cannot be achieved<br><b>Example:</b> His plan to become a millionaire overnight is just pie in the sky.	
Piece of Cake	<b>Bengali:</b> খুব সহজে সম্পন্ন<br><b>English:</b> Very easily done<br><b>Example:</b> The exam was a piece of cake - I finished in 30 minutes.	
Pin Someone Down	<b>Bengali:</b> সিদ্ধান্ত বা স্পষ্ট উত্তরের দাবি<br><b>English:</b> Demand a decision or clear answer<br><b>Example:</b> I tried to pin him down on a delivery date, but he was evasive.	
Pinch Pennies	<b>Bengali:</b> অর্থের সাথে সতর্ক থাকা, মিতব্যয়ী হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> To be careful with money, to be thrifty<br><b>Example:</b> Since losing his job, he's been pinching pennies to make ends meet.	
Pink Slip	<b>Bengali:</b> ছাঁটাইয়ের নোটিস; চাকরি হারানো, সাধারণত ছাঁটাইয়ের কারণে<br><b>English:</b> A layoff notice; loss of a job, typically because of layoffs<br><b>Example:</b> Many employees got pink slips when the company downsized.	
Pipe Dream	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি অবাস্তব আশা, একটি কল্পনা<br><b>English:</b> An unrealistic hope, a fantasy<br><b>Example:</b> Winning the lottery is just a pipe dream for most people.	
Piping Hot	<b>Bengali:</b> খুবই গরম (সাধারণত খাবারের ক্ষেত্রে বলা হয়)<br><b>English:</b> Very hot (generally said of food)<br><b>Example:</b> Be careful - that soup is piping hot.	
Pipped to the Post	<b>Bengali:</b> সামান্য ব্যবধানে পরাজিত<br><b>English:</b> Defeated by a narrow margin<br><b>Example:</b> He was pipped to the post in the final seconds of the race.	
Pissing Contest	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি অর্থহীন তর্ক বা প্রতিযোগিতা, সাধারণত পুরুষদের মধ্যে<br><b>English:</b> A meaningless argument or competition, typically between males<br><b>Example:</b> Their argument about whose car is faster is just a pissing contest.	
Play Ball	<b>Bengali:</b> সহযোগিতা করা, অংশগ্রহণে সম্মত হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Cooperate, agree to participate<br><b>Example:</b> If you want this deal to work, you need to play ball.	
Play Cat And Mouse	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে ভুল করাতে প্রতারণা করার চেষ্টা যাতে তাদের পরাজিত করা যায়<br><b>English:</b> Trying to trick someone into making a mistake so you can defeat them<br><b>Example:</b> The detective played cat and mouse with the suspect during questioning.	
Play Hardball	<b>Bengali:</b> কঠোর আলোচনার অবস্থান গ্রহণ করা; আক্রমণাত্মকভাবে কাজ করা<br><b>English:</b> Adopt a tough negotiating position; act aggressively<br><b>Example:</b> When the union wouldn't budge, management decided to play hardball.	
Play It by Ear	<b>Bengali:</b> নির্দিষ্ট পরিকল্পনার পরিবর্তে পরিস্থিতি অনুযায়ী সাড়া দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> To respond to circumstances instead of having a fixed plan<br><b>Example:</b> We don't have reservations, so we'll just play it by ear.	
Play the Percentages	<b>Bengali:</b> যা ঘটার সম্ভাবনা সবচেয়ে বেশি তার উপর বাজি ধরা বা নির্ভর করা<br><b>English:</b> Bet on or rely on what is most likely to happen<br><b>Example:</b> The coach plays the percentages by using his best players in crucial moments.	
Play the Ponies	<b>Bengali:</b> ঘোড়দৌড়ে বাজি ধরা<br><b>English:</b> Bet on horse racing<br><b>Example:</b> Every weekend, he goes to the track to play the ponies.	
Play With Fire	<b>Bengali:</b> খুবই ঝুঁকিপূর্ণ কিছু করা<br><b>English:</b> Do something very risky<br><b>Example:</b> Dating your boss is playing with fire.	
Play Your Cards Right	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি পরিস্থিতিকে নিজের সর্বোচ্চ সুবিধার জন্য কাজে লাগানো<br><b>English:</b> Exploit a situation to your best advantage<br><b>Example:</b> If you play your cards right, you could get that promotion.	
Point of No Return	<b>Bengali:</b> এমন জায়গা যেখান থেকে শুরুর স্থানে ফিরে যাওয়া অসম্ভব<br><b>English:</b> A place from which it is impossible to go back to the starting point<br><b>Example:</b> Once we sign the contract, we'll reach the point of no return.	
Point the Finger At	<b>Bengali:</b> (কাউকে) দোষারোপ করা<br><b>English:</b> Blame (someone)<br><b>Example:</b> Don't point the finger at me - you made the mistake too.	
Poison Pill	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি ব্যবস্থা বা সত্তাকে কম আকর্ষণীয় করার জন্য যোগ করা বিধান বা বৈশিষ্ট্য, একটি অবাঞ্ছিত সংযোজন<br><b>English:</b> A provision or feature added to a measure or an entity to make it less attractive, an undesirable add-on<br><b>Example:</b> The company added a poison pill to prevent the hostile takeover.	
Pop One's Clogs	<b>Bengali:</b> মৃত্যুবরণ করা<br><b>English:</b> To die<br><b>Example:</b> The old man finally popped his clogs at age 95.	
Pop One's Cork	<b>Bengali:</b> রাগ প্রকাশ করা; রেগে যাওয়া<br><b>English:</b> To release one's anger; to blow one's top<br><b>Example:</b> He popped his cork when he saw the damage to his car.	
Pop the Question	<b>Bengali:</b> বিবাহের প্রস্তাব দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Propose marriage<br><b>Example:</b> After dating for three years, he finally popped the question.	
Pot Calling the Kettle Black	<b>Bengali:</b> এমন কিছুর জন্য কাউকে অভিযুক্ত করা যার জন্য নিজেও দোষী; ভণ্ডামি করা<br><b>English:</b> Accusing someone of something of which you are also guilty; being hypocritical<br><b>Example:</b> Him calling me lazy is the pot calling the kettle black - he never does any work.	
Pour (Rub) Salt into (on) the Wound	<b>Bengali:</b> অপমান বা আঘাত আরো খারাপ করা; কারো খারাপ পরিস্থিতি আরো খারাপ করা<br><b>English:</b> Worsen an insult or injury; make a bad situation worse for someone<br><b>Example:</b> Mentioning his ex-girlfriend was pouring salt into the wound.	
Powder Keg	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি বিস্ফোরক পরিস্থিতি, এমন পরিস্থিতি যেখানে মানুষ রাগান্বিত এবং হিংসাত্মক হতে প্রস্তুত<br><b>English:</b> An explosive situation, a situation in which people are angry and ready to be violent<br><b>Example:</b> The protest was a powder keg waiting to explode.	
Powder One's Nose	<b>Bengali:</b> বাথরুম ব্যবহার করা। এটি মহিলারা ব্যবহার করেন<br><b>English:</b> To use the restroom (lavatory). This is used by women<br><b>Example:</b> Excuse me, I need to powder my nose before the meeting.	
Preach to the Choir	<b>Bengali:</b> এমন যুক্তি দেওয়া যার সাথে আপনার শ্রোতারা ইতিমধ্যে একমত<br><b>English:</b> To make an argument with which your listeners already agree<br><b>Example:</b> Telling environmentalists about climate change is preaching to the choir.	
Pretty Penny	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রচুর অর্থ; অত্যধিক অর্থ (কিছুর দামের কথা বলার সময়)<br><b>English:</b> A lot of money; too much money (when referring to the cost of something)<br><b>Example:</b> That designer dress must have cost a pretty penny.	
Price Yourself Out of the Market	<b>Bengali:</b> এত বেশি দামে পণ্য বা সেবা বিক্রি করার চেষ্টা করা যে কেউ কিনে না<br><b>English:</b> Try to sell goods or services at such a high price that nobody buys them<br><b>Example:</b> If you charge too much for consulting, you'll price yourself out of the market.	
Puddle Jumper	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি ছোট বিমান, ছোট ভ্রমণে ব্যবহৃত<br><b>English:</b> A small airplane, used on short trips<br><b>Example:</b> We took a puddle jumper from the main airport to the island.	
Pull Out All the Stops	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু সম্পন্ন করার জন্য সবকিছু সম্ভব করা<br><b>English:</b> Do everything possible to accomplish something<br><b>Example:</b> For their wedding, they pulled out all the stops.	
Pull Strings	<b>Bengali:</b> ব্যক্তিগত সংযোগের ভিত্তিতে প্রভাব ব্যবহার করা<br><b>English:</b> Use influence that's based on personal connections<br><b>Example:</b> He pulled strings to get his son into that exclusive school.	
Pull the Plug On	<b>Bengali:</b> (কিছু) বন্ধ করে দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Terminate (something)<br><b>Example:</b> The network pulled the plug on the TV show after poor ratings.	
Pull Yourself Together	<b>Bengali:</b> আপনার আবেগ নিয়ন্ত্রণ করুন; প্রবল আবেগিক বিপর্যয় থেকে সেরে উঠুন<br><b>English:</b> Control your emotions; recover from a strong emotional upset<br><b>Example:</b> Pull yourself together - crying won't solve anything.	
Puppies And Rainbows	<b>Bengali:</b> নিখুঁত, আদর্শ (সাধারণত সামান্য ব্যঙ্গাত্মকভাবে ব্যবহৃত, কম আদর্শ পরিস্থিতির বিপরীতে)<br><b>English:</b> Perfect, ideal (usually used slightly sarcastically, in contrast with a less ideal situation)<br><b>Example:</b> Life isn't all puppies and rainbows - there are real problems to face.	
Puppy Dog Eyes	<b>Bengali:</b> অনুনয়ের দৃষ্টি<br><b>English:</b> A begging look<br><b>Example:</b> She gave him puppy dog eyes until he agreed to take her shopping.	
Puppy Love	<b>Bengali:</b> কিশোর প্রেম বা মোহ, বিশেষ করে যা দীর্ঘস্থায়ী হওয়ার প্রত্যাশা নেই<br><b>English:</b> Adolescent love or infatuation, especially one that is not expected to last<br><b>Example:</b> Their teenage romance was just puppy love.	
Pure as the Driven Snow	<b>Bengali:</b> নিষ্পাপ এবং পবিত্র হওয়া (প্রায়ই ব্যঙ্গাত্মকভাবে ব্যবহৃত)<br><b>English:</b> To be innocent and chaste (frequently used ironically)<br><b>Example:</b> She acts like she's pure as the driven snow, but we know better.	
Push the Envelope	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছু করার সাধারণ উপায়ের বাইরে যাওয়া, উদ্ভাবনী হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Go beyond common ways of doing something, be innovative<br><b>Example:</b> The artist likes to push the envelope with controversial subjects.	
Pushing Up Daisies	<b>Bengali:</b> মৃত এবং সমাধিস্থ<br><b>English:</b> Dead and buried<br><b>Example:</b> By the time that investment pays off, I'll be pushing up daisies.Front	
Let Sleeping Dogs Lie	<b>Bengali:</b> সমস্যায় নাড়াচাড়া এড়ানো; বিষয়গুলো একা ছেড়ে দেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> To avoid stirring up a problem; to leave things alone<br><b>Example:</b> I know you're curious about their divorce, but let sleeping dogs lie.	duplicate
Let the Cat Out of the Bag	<b>Bengali:</b> একটি গোপনীয়তা প্রকাশ করা, সাধারণত এমন গোপনীয়তা যা আপনি বা অন্যরা লুকিয়ে রাখার চেষ্টা করছেন<br><b>English:</b> Reveal a secret, usually a secret you or others are trying to keep<br><b>Example:</b> Don't let the cat out of the bag about the surprise party.	duplicate
Let the Genie Out of the Bottle	<b>Bengali:</b> এতদিন দমিয়ে রাখা কিছু প্রকাশ করা<br><b>English:</b> Reveal something hitherto suppressed<br><b>Example:</b> Once nuclear weapons were invented, we let the genie out of the bottle.	duplicate
Letter of the Law	<b>Bengali:</b> আইনের স্পষ্ট অর্থ, আইনের মূল উদ্দেশ্যের বিপরীতে<br><b>English:</b> The explicit meaning of a law, as opposed to the spirit of the law<br><b>Example:</b> He follows the letter of the law but ignores its spirit.	duplicate
Lick One's Wounds	<b>Bengali:</b> খারাপ পরাজয়ের পর বিশ্রাম নেওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Rest after a bad defeat<br><b>Example:</b> After losing the election, he went home to lick his wounds.	duplicate
Life is A Bowl of Cherries	<b>Bengali:</b> জীবন চমৎকার বা খুবই আনন্দদায়ক<br><b>English:</b> Life is wonderful or very pleasant<br><b>Example:</b> When you're young and healthy, life is a bowl of cherries.	duplicate
Light a Fire Under Someone	<b>Bengali:</b> কাউকে কঠিন পরিশ্রম করতে অনুপ্রাণিত করা<br><b>English:</b> Inspire someone to work very hard<br><b>Example:</b> The coach lit a fire under the team during halftime.	duplicate
Light at the End of the Tunnel	<b>Bengali:</b> দীর্ঘ কষ্টের পর আশার আলো<br><b>English:</b> A sign of hope after a long period of difficulties<br><b>Example:</b> After months of unemployment, the job interview was light at the end of the tunnel.	duplicate
Like a Kid in a Candy Store	<b>Bengali:</b> পরিবেশ নিয়ে এতটাই উত্তেজিত হওয়া যে শিশুর মতো বা বোকার মতো আচরণ করা<br><b>English:</b> To be so excited about one's surroundings that one acts in a childlike or silly way<br><b>Example:</b> At the electronics store, he was like a kid in a candy store.	duplicate
Like a Moth to a Flame	<b>Bengali:</b> বিপদ সত্ত্বেও কিছু বা কারো প্রতি আকৃষ্ট হওয়া<br><b>English:</b> Drawn to something or someone despite the dangers<br><b>Example:</b> He's drawn to risky investments like a moth to a flame.	duplicate
Like Father, Like Son	<b>Bengali:</b> ছেলেরা তাদের বাবার বৈশিষ্ট্য ও পছন্দ উত্তরাধিকার সূত্রে পায়, প্রায়ই না বুঝেই<br><b>English:</b> Sons inherit their fathers' traits and preferences, often even without realizing it<br><b>Example:</b> Both father and son are doctors - like father, like son.	duplicate
Like Shooting Fish in a Barrel	<b>Bengali:</b> অত্যন্ত সহজ<br><b>English:</b> Very easy<br><b>Example:</b> Beating that weak team was like shooting fish in a barrel.	duplicate
Like Taking Candy from a Baby	<b>Bengali:</b> অত্যন্ত সহজ<br><b>English:</b> Very easy<br><b>Example:</b> The exam was like taking candy from a baby.	duplicate
Like The Cat That Got The Cream	<b>Bengali:</b> বিশেষভাবে আত্মতুষ্ট দেখানো, প্রায়ই অন্যদের বিরক্তির কারণ<br><b>English:</b> Looking particularly self-satisfied, often to the annoyance of others<br><b>Example:</b> After getting the promotion, he looked like the cat that got the cream.	duplicate
Like Two Peas in a Pod	<b>Bengali:</b> প্রবল মিল থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Bearing a strong resemblance<br><b>Example:</b> The twins are like two peas in a pod - you can't tell them apart.	duplicate
Lion's Den	<b>Bengali:</b> যেকোনো বিপজ্জনক বা ভয়ানক জায়গা<br><b>English:</b> Any dangerous or frightening place<br><b>Example:</b> Walking into that hostile board meeting was like entering the lion's den.	duplicate
Lion's Share	<b>Bengali:</b> কিছুর সবচেয়ে বড় অংশ<br><b>English:</b> The largest part of something<br><b>Example:</b> The CEO gets the lion's share of the company's profits.	duplicate
Live Large	<b>Bengali:</b> বিলাসবহুল জীবনযাত্রা<br><b>English:</b> Have a luxurious lifestyle<br><b>Example:</b> After winning the lottery, they decided to live large.	duplicate
Living in Cloud Cuckooland	<b>Bengali:</b> অবাস্তব বা বোকামি বিশ্বাস বা পরিকল্পনা থাকা<br><b>English:</b> Having unrealistic or foolish beliefs or plans<br><b>Example:</b> If you think you'll get rich without working, you're living in cloud cuckooland.	duplicate
Living on Borrowed Time	<b>Bengali:</b> অসুস্থতা বা মৃত্যুর কাছাকাছি অভিজ্ঞতার পর, অনেকে বিশ্বাস করে তারা মৃত্যুকে ঠকিয়েছে<br><b>English:</b> Following an illness or near-death experience, many people believe they have cheated death<br><b>Example:</b> After the heart attack, he felt like he was living on borrowed time.	duplicate
Living Under a Rock	<b>Bengali:</b> গুরুত্বপূর্ণ ঘটনা সম্পর্কে অজ্ঞ। সাধারণত প্রশ্ন হিসেবে ব্যবহৃত<br><b>English:</b> Ignorant of important events. Usually used as a question: Have you been living under a rock?<br><b>Example:</b> You don't know about the election results? Have you been living under a rock?	duplicate
Loaded for Bear	<b>Bengali:</b> সমস্যার জন্য প্রস্তুত, চ্যালেঞ্জের জন্য ভালভাবে প্রস্তুত<br><b>English:</b> Prepared for problems, well prepared for a challenge<br><b>Example:</b> The lawyer came to court loaded for bear with evidence.	duplicate
